

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/ToolContainerService.lua ---

--[[
    ToolContainerService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Tool Container Service
-- Khizzer
-- May 5, 2023

local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
local ServerStorage = game:GetService('ServerStorage');

local CarService;
local NetworkService;
local ProfileDataService;
local CheckLEO;
local WebUtil;
local NotificationService;

local ToolContainerService = {Client = {}}

type ToolContainer = {
    Type: "Player" | "Bin" | "Car";
    Instance: Instance;
}
local CarContainers;
local BinContainers;

local CANNOT_SAVE = {"Protest Sign", "Tire Pump", "Delete", "Placeable Identifier", "Building Tools", "F3X", "Fists"};

local IGNORED_ATTRIBUTES = {"Welded", "CanBreakWindows"}

function ToolContainerService:_setupToolContainers()
    local ToolContainers = Instance.new('Folder');
    ToolContainers.Name = 'ToolContainers';
    ToolContainers.Parent = ServerStorage;

    CarContainers = Instance.new('Folder');
    CarContainers.Name = 'CarContainers';
    CarContainers.Parent = ToolContainers;

    BinContainers = Instance.new('Folder');
    BinContainers.Name = 'BinContainers';
    BinContainers.Parent = ToolContainers;

    for _,v in next, ServerStorage:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Tool') then
            v:SetAttribute('DoNotSave', true);
        end;
    end;

    for _,v in next, workspace.Bins:GetChildren() do
        self:CreateContainerForInstance(v);
    end;
end;

function ToolContainerService:_getContainerFromInstance(instance: Instance)
    if not typeof(instance) == "Instance" then return; end;

    if instance.Parent == workspace.Bins then
        for _,v in next, BinContainers:GetChildren() do
            if v:FindFirstChild('Bin') and v.Bin.Value == instance then
                return v;
            end;
        end;
    elseif instance.Parent == workspace.Cars then
        for _,v in next, CarContainers:GetChildren() do
            if v:FindFirstChild('Car') and v.Car.Value == instance then
                return v;
            end;
        end;
    elseif instance.Parent == game.Players then
        return instance.Backpack;
    end;
end;

function ToolContainerService:_scanBin(bin, tbl)
    for _,v in next, BinContainers:GetChildren() do
        if v:FindFirstChild('Bin') and v.Bin.Value == bin then
            for _,v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                if v2:IsA('Tool') then
                    table.insert(tbl, {Name = v2.Name});
                end;
            end;
            break;
        end;
    end;
end

function ToolContainerService:_scanCar(car, tbl)
    for _,v in next, CarContainers:GetChildren() do
        if v:FindFirstChild('Car') and v.Car.Value == car then
            for _,v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                if v2:IsA('Tool') then
                    table.insert(tbl, {Name = v2.Name});
                end;
            end;
            break;
        end;
    end
end

function ToolContainerService:_canPlayerDeal(plr: Player)
    return (plr.Team.Name ~= "Civilian" and plr.Team.Name ~= "Prisoner") or (plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil);
end;

--Car is only used for emergency vehicles (temp storage instead of data saving)
function ToolContainerService:CreateContainerForInstance(instance: Instance)
    if instance.Parent == workspace.Bins then
        local binContainer = Instance.new('Folder');
        binContainer.Name = instance.Name;
        binContainer.Parent = BinContainers;

        local objectValue = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        objectValue.Name = 'Bin';
        objectValue.Value = instance;
        objectValue.Parent = binContainer;

        return binContainer;
    elseif instance.Parent == workspace.Cars then
        local carContainer = Instance.new('Folder');
        carContainer.Name = instance.Name;
        carContainer.Parent = CarContainers;

        local objectValue = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        objectValue.Name = 'Car';
        objectValue.Value = instance;
        objectValue.Parent = carContainer;

        instance.Destroying:Once(function()
            carContainer:Destroy();
        end);
        return carContainer;
    end;
end;

function ToolContainerService:Start()
    self:_setupToolContainers();

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('CanOpenTrunk', function(plr: Player, data: ToolContainer)
        if data.Type ~= "Car" then return; end;
        if typeof(data.Instance) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
        if data.Instance.Parent ~= workspace.Cars then return; end;

        local car = data.Instance;

        if plr.Character:GetAttribute("HandcuffedBy") then return end
        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return end
        if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - car.Body.Trunk.Position).Magnitude > 7 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Move closer to the vehicle.');
            return;
        end;

        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

        if not CheckLEO(plr) and car:GetAttribute('Owner') ~= plr.Name and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;

        local suspectPlr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(car:GetAttribute('Owner'));
        if not suspectPlr then return; end;

        if CheckLEO(plr) and CarService.IsCivilianCar(car) then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'OfficerTrunkSearch', suspectPlr);
            NetworkService.Send(suspectPlr, 'SuspectTrunkSearch', plr);
            return {
                CanOpen = false;
                ConsentNeeded = true;
            };
        end;

        return {
            CanOpen = true;
            ConsentNeeded = false;
        };
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('ConsentTrunkSearch', function(plr: Player, officer: Player)
        if not CheckLEO(officer) then return; end;

        NetworkService.Send(officer, 'ConsentTrunkSearch');
    end)

	NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetToolContainer', function(plr, data: ToolContainer)
        if data.Type == "Bin" then
            local bin = data.Instance;

            if bin == nil then return; end;
            if typeof(bin) ~= "Instance" then return; end;

            if bin.Parent ~= workspace.Bins then return; end;

            if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - bin.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;
            local dataToSend = {};

            self:_scanBin(bin, dataToSend);
            return dataToSend;

        elseif data.Type == "Car" then
            local car = data.Instance;

            if car == nil then return; end;
            if typeof(car) ~= "Instance" then return; end;

            if car.Parent ~= workspace.Cars then return; end;

            if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - car.Body.Trunk.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

            if CarService.IsEmergencyCar(car) then
                local dataToSend = {};

                self:_scanCar(car, dataToSend);

                return dataToSend;
            else
                local carOwner = car:GetAttribute('Owner');

                if not carOwner then return; end; --Developer cars

                local carOwnerPlr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(carOwner);
                if not carOwnerPlr then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'Car owner is not in game.'); end;

                for _,vehicle in next, ProfileDataService.GetData(carOwnerPlr, 'BoughtCars') do
                    if tonumber(vehicle.ID) == car.Config.ID.Value then
                        return vehicle.Inventory or {};
                    end;
                end;
            end
        elseif data.Type == "Player" then
            local suspectPlr = data.Instance;
            if typeof(suspectPlr) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
            if suspectPlr:IsA('Player') ~= true then return; end;

            local dataToSend = {};

            for _,v in next, suspectPlr:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    table.insert(dataToSend, {Name = v.Name});
                end
            end;

            return dataToSend;
        end
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('SwapFromToolContainer', function(plr: Player, toolName: string, sourceContainer: ToolContainer, destinationContainer: ToolContainer)
        if typeof(sourceContainer.Instance) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
        if typeof(destinationContainer.Instance) ~= "Instance" then return; end;

        if game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0 and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450 then
            return _G.AeroError(plr, 'Tool containers are disabled in private servers.');
        end;

        if plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 1 then return; end;

        if sourceContainer.Type == 'Player' then
            if not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName) then return; end;

            do
                local tool = plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName);
                if tool:GetAttribute('DoNotSave') then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'This tool cannot be transferred'); end;
            end;
            if destinationContainer.Type == 'Bin' then
                --From player to bin
                local bin = destinationContainer.Instance;

                if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - bin.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;
                if bin.Parent ~= workspace.Bins then return; end;

                local tool = plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName);
                if not tool then return; end;

                local spacelimit = bin:GetAttribute('Space') or 50;
                if #self:_getContainerFromInstance(bin):GetChildren() > spacelimit then
                    _G.AeroError(plr, `This container is full. It can only hold {spacelimit} items`);
                    tool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
                    return;
                end;
                tool.Parent = self:_getContainerFromInstance(bin);

                local attributes = tool:GetAttributes();

                if self:_canPlayerDeal(plr) then
                    if tool:GetAttribute('ToolSource') then
                        WebUtil.SendWebhook("https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1106894404385525800/-xwPaCYeRmPMEybF5ywfbPL_BiWP26vgEKFitvW5GCA_twB2cabWjmPYVw2v3MevErFY", 1106893684349349898 , {
                            embeds = {
                                {
                                    title = "Officer placed tool in bin",
                                    fields = {
                                        {
                                            name = "Tool Name",
                                            value = toolName
                                        },
                                        {
                                            name = "Tool Attributes",
                                            value = HttpService:JSONEncode(attributes)
                                        },
                                        {
                                            name = "Officer",
                                            value = plr.Name
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        })
                    end
                end;
            elseif destinationContainer.Type == 'Car' then
                --From player to trunk

                local car = destinationContainer.Instance;
                local carOwner = car:GetAttribute('Owner');

                if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - car.Body.Trunk.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'Move closer to the car.'); end;

                if table.find(CANNOT_SAVE ,toolName) then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'This tool cannot be saved.'); end;
                if not carOwner or car:GetAttribute("SpawnedCar") then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'This car cannot have items stored in it.'); end; --Developer cars

                if CarService.IsEmergencyCar(car) then
                    plr.Backpack[toolName].Parent = self:_getContainerFromInstance(car);

                    local carOwnerPlr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(carOwner);
                    if CheckLEO(plr) and plr ~= carOwnerPlr then
                        NotificationService.Send(carOwnerPlr, 'Trunk Placement', `{plr.Name} has placed {toolName} in your {car.Name}'s trunk.`);
                    end;
                else
                    local carOwnerPlr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(carOwner);
                    if not carOwnerPlr then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'Car owner is not in game.'); end;

                    if carOwnerPlr ~= plr and not CheckLEO(plr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;

                    local tool = plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName);
                    if not tool then return; end;

                    local attributes = tool:GetAttributes();

                    tool.Parent = ServerStorage;

                    local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(carOwnerPlr, 'BoughtCars');
                    for _,vehicle in next, carData do
                        if tonumber(vehicle.ID) == car.Config.ID.Value then
                            if not vehicle.Inventory then
                                vehicle.Inventory = {};
                            end;
                            local trunkLimit = car:GetAttribute('TrunkSpace') or 25;
                            if #vehicle.Inventory > trunkLimit then
                                _G.AeroError(plr, `This car's trunk is full. It can only hold {trunkLimit} items`);
                                tool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
                                return;
                            end;
                            tool:Destroy();
                            table.insert(vehicle.Inventory, {
                                Name = toolName;
                                Attributes = attributes
                            });
                            ProfileDataService.SetData(carOwnerPlr, 'BoughtCars', carData);
                            if self:_canPlayerDeal(plr) and tool:GetAttribute('ToolSource') then
                                if CheckLEO(plr) then
                                    NotificationService.Send(carOwnerPlr, 'Trunk Placement', `{plr.Name} has placed {toolName} in your {car.Name}'s trunk.`);
                                end

                                WebUtil.SendWebhook("https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1106894404385525800/-xwPaCYeRmPMEybF5ywfbPL_BiWP26vgEKFitvW5GCA_twB2cabWjmPYVw2v3MevErFY", 1106893684349349898 , {
                                    embeds = {
                                        {
                                            title = "Officer placed tool in trunk",
                                            fields = {
                                                {
                                                    name = "Tool Name",
                                                    value = toolName
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    name = "Tool Attributes",
                                                    value = HttpService:JSONEncode(attributes)
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    name = "Officer",
                                                    value = plr.Name
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    name = "Suspect",
                                                    value = carOwnerPlr.Name
                                                },
                                                {
                                                    name = "Car",
                                                    value = `ID = {car.Config.ID.Value} ({car.Name})`
                                                }
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                })
                            end;
                            break;
                        end;
                    end;
                end
            elseif destinationContainer.Type == 'Player' then
                --From player to another player (officer giving to suspect)
                local sourcePlr = sourceContainer.Instance;
                local destinationPlr = destinationContainer.Instance;

                if typeof(sourcePlr) ~= "Instance" then return; end;
                if typeof(destinationPlr) ~= "Instance" then return; end;

                if sourcePlr:IsA('Player') ~= true then return; end;
                if destinationPlr:IsA('Player') ~= true then return; end;

                if sourcePlr == destinationPlr then return; end;

                if (sourcePlr ~= plr) and (destinationPlr ~= plr) then return; end;

                local checkLEO = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO;

                if not checkLEO(plr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;

                if sourcePlr == plr then
                    --If the officer is giving it to the suspect
                    if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - destinationPlr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;
                    if destinationPlr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= plr.Name then return; end;
                    if destinationPlr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= sourcePlr.Name then return; end;

                    if not checkLEO(sourcePlr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;

                    local _tool = sourcePlr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName);
                    if not _tool then return; end;

                    _tool.Parent = destinationPlr;
                elseif destinationPlr == plr then
                    --If the officer is taking it from the suspect
                    if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - sourcePlr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;
                    if sourcePlr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= plr.Name then return; end;
                    if sourcePlr:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= destinationPlr.Name then return; end;

                    if not checkLEO(destinationPlr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;

                    local _tool = sourcePlr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(toolName);
                    if not _tool then return; end;

                    _tool.Parent = plr;
                end
            end
        elseif sourceContainer.Type == 'Bin' then
            --From bin to player
            local bin = sourceContainer.Instance;

            if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - bin.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;

            local container = self:_getContainerFromInstance(bin);

            local targetTool = container:FindFirstChild(toolName);
            if not targetTool then return; end;

            targetTool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
        elseif sourceContainer.Type == 'Car' then
            --From trunk to player
            local car = sourceContainer.Instance;
            if (plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position - car.Body.Trunk.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;
            local carOwner = car:GetAttribute('Owner');
            local carOwnerPlr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(carOwner);

            if CarService.IsEmergencyCar(car) then
                local container = self:_getContainerFromInstance(car);

                local targetTool = container:FindFirstChild(toolName);
                if not targetTool then return; end;

                targetTool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
            else
                local carOwner = car:GetAttribute('Owner');

                if not carOwner then return; end; --Developer cars

                local carOwnerPlr = game.Players:FindFirstChild(carOwner);
                if not carOwnerPlr then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'Car owner is not in game.'); end;

                if carOwnerPlr ~= plr and not CheckLEO(plr) and plr:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" then return; end;
                local carData = ProfileDataService.GetData(carOwnerPlr, 'BoughtCars');
                for _,vehicle in next, carData do
                    if tonumber(vehicle.ID) == car.Config.ID.Value then
                        for i,v in next, vehicle.Inventory do
                            if v.Name == toolName then
                                table.remove(vehicle.Inventory, i);
                                ProfileDataService.SetData(carOwnerPlr, 'BoughtCars', carData);
                                local targetTool = game.ServerStorage:FindFirstChild(toolName) or self.ServerAssets.BusinessTools:FindFirstChild(toolName, true);
                                if not targetTool then return; end;
                                if v.Attributes.Variant and ServerStorage.ToolVariants:FindFirstChild(toolName) then
                                    targetTool = ServerStorage.ToolVariants[toolName]:FindFirstChild(v.Attributes.Variant) or targetTool
                                end

                                local newTool = targetTool:Clone();
                                newTool.Name = toolName;
                                newTool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
                                for i2,v2 in next, v.Attributes do
                                    if not table.find(IGNORED_ATTRIBUTES, i2) then
                                        newTool:SetAttribute(i2, v2);
                                    end;
                                end;
                                newTool:SetAttribute('DoNotSave', nil);
                                break;
                            end;
                        end;
                        break;
                    end;
                end;
            end
            if CheckLEO(plr) and plr ~= carOwnerPlr then
                NotificationService.Send(carOwnerPlr, 'Trunk Removal', `{plr.Name} has removed {toolName} from your {car.Name}'s trunk.`);
            end;
        end
    end)
end


function ToolContainerService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    CarService = self.Services.CarService;
    ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
    CheckLEO = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO;
    WebUtil = self.Modules.WebUtil;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
end


return ToolContainerService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/BatonService.lua ---

--[[
    BatonService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local BREAK_SOUND_ID = 'rbxassetid://4757900430';

local BatonService = {Client = {}};
local DamageCharacter;

function BatonService:Start()
    self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('Baton', function(plr, event, hit)
        if (plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - hit.Position).Magnitude > 8 then return; end;

        if not typeof(hit) == "Instance" then return; end;

        local baton = plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool');
        if not baton then return; end;
        if not baton:GetAttribute('Module') == 'Baton' then return; end;

        if event == 'CharacterHit' then
            local humanoid = hit.Parent.Humanoid;
            DamageCharacter(humanoid.Parent, 5, plr);
            humanoid.Sit = true;
        elseif event == 'BreakableGlassHit' then
            local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
            breakSound.SoundId = BREAK_SOUND_ID;
            breakSound.Volume = 0.6;
            breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
            breakSound.Parent = hit;
            hit:Destroy();
        end;
    end);
end;

function BatonService:Init()
    DamageCharacter = self.Modules.DamageCharacter;
end;

return BatonService;

--[[
    FireHoseService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools

-- Fire Hose Service
-- Khizzer
-- July 2, 2021

local NetworkService;

local FireHoseService = {Client = {}, HoseConnections = {}}

local EXTINGUISH_EVENT;
local SPRAY_EVENT;
local ATTACH_ATTACK_LINE_EVENT;
local ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TRUCK_EVENT;
local ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TANK_EVENT;
local DESTROY_SPRING_CONNECTION_EVENT;

local ATTACK_LINE;

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');
local PathfindingService = game:GetService('PathfindingService')
local PhysicsService = game:GetService('PhysicsService');

function updateWaterDisplay(waterDisplay)
    local waterCapacity = waterDisplay.Parent.Parent.Config:FindFirstChild('WaterCapacity');
    for _,SurfaceGui in pairs(waterDisplay:GetChildren()) do
        if SurfaceGui:IsA('SurfaceGui') then
            SurfaceGui.MainFrame.WaterBarImage.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, waterCapacity.Value / 100, 0);
        end;
    end;
end

function setChildrenTransparency(parent, transparency)
    for _,child in next, parent:GetChildren() do
        if child:IsA('BasePart') and not string.find(child.Name, 'r1') and not string.find(child.Name, 'r2') then
            child.Transparency = transparency;
        end;
    end;
end;

function scanForFire(house)
    for _,v in next, house:GetDescendants() do
        if v:IsA('Fire') then
            return true;
        end;
    end;
end;

--[[ local function joinTwoParts(part1: BasePart, part2: BasePart)
    local direction = part1.CFrame.LookVector

    part2.CFrame = part1.CFrame * CFrame.new(direction * part1.Size.Z)

    local frontAttachment = part1.Front;
    local backAttachment = part2.Back;

    part1.BallSocketConstraint.Attachment0 = frontAttachment;
    part1.BallSocketConstraint.Attachment1 = backAttachment;

    local partBefore = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
    partBefore.Name = 'PartBefore';
    partBefore.Value = part1;
    partBefore.Parent = part2;

    local partAfter = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
    partAfter.Name = 'PartAfter';
    partAfter.Value = part2;
    partAfter.Parent = part1;
end;

local longestSide = math.max(workspace.HosePart.Size.X, workspace.HosePart.Size.Y, workspace.HosePart.Size.Z);

local function createHose(source: BasePart, destination: BasePart)
    local path = PathfindingService:CreatePath({
        WaypointSpacing = longestSide - 0.1
    });

    local lastHosePart = workspace.HosePart:Clone();
    lastHosePart.Parent = workspace;
    lastHosePart.Position = source.Position;
    lastHosePart.Anchored = true;

    joinTwoParts(source, lastHosePart);
    lastHosePart.PartBefore:Destroy(); --Makes sure the fire truck interaction part isnt counted in getPartCount()

    path:ComputeAsync(lastHosePart.Position, destination.Position);

    local waypoints = path:GetWaypoints();
    if path.Status == Enum.PathStatus.Success then
        print('Success');
        for i,v in next, waypoints do
            local partCount = math.abs(math.floor((v.Position - lastHosePart.Position).Magnitude / longestSide));
            if partCount > 0 then
                for j = 1, partCount do
                    local hosePart = workspace.HosePart:Clone();
                    hosePart.Parent = workspace;
                    hosePart.Position = lastHosePart.Position + (v.Position - lastHosePart.Position).Unit * longestSide * i;
                    joinTwoParts(lastHosePart, hosePart);
                    hosePart.Anchored = false;
                    lastHosePart = hosePart;
                end;
            end;
        end;

        joinTwoParts(lastHosePart, destination);

        return lastHosePart
    elseif path.Status == Enum.PathStatus.NoPath then
        print('No path')
    end;
end; ]]


function FireHoseService:Start()
    PhysicsService:RegisterCollisionGroup('FireHose');
    PhysicsService:CollisionGroupSetCollidable('Default', 'FireHose', false);

    NetworkService.Connect(EXTINGUISH_EVENT, function(plr, part)
        if not plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Attack Line') then return; end;
        if not part:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') and not part:FindFirstChildOfClass('Fire') then return; end;
        
        if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment') then
--[[             local health = part.Attachment.Fire:GetAttribute('Health');
            part.Attachment.Fire:SetAttribute('Health' , health - 10);
            if part.Attachment.Fire:GetAttribute('Health') <= 0 then ]]
                part.Attachment:Destroy();
--[[             end; ]]
        else
            part:FindFirstChildOfClass('Fire'):Destroy();
        end
        --local house = HouseService:getHouseFromPart(part);
        --local onFire = scanForFire(house.HouseModel)
        --if not onFire then
        --    house:SetOffFire();
        --end;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect(SPRAY_EVENT, function(plr, tool)
        if not typeof(tool) == 'Instance' then return; end;

        local waterCapacity = tool.WaterCapacity.Value;
        waterCapacity.Value = waterCapacity.Value - 0.01;
        local waterDisplay = waterCapacity.Parent.Parent.Body.WaterDisplay;
        updateWaterDisplay(waterDisplay);
    end)

--[[     NetworkService.Connect(ATTACH_ATTACK_LINE_EVENT, function(plr, interactionPart)
        local hoseToolPart = plr.Character['Attack Line'].LineEnd;

        local lastHosePart = createHose(interactionPart, hoseToolPart);

        local function getPartCount(lastPart: BasePart, count: number): number
            local partBefore = lastPart:FindFirstChild('PartBefore');
            if partBefore then
                count += 1;
                return getPartCount(partBefore.Value, count)
            else
                return count;
            end;
        end;

        task.spawn(function()
            while true do
                local path = PathfindingService:CreatePath({
                    WaypointSpacing = longestSide - 0.15
                });

                path:ComputeAsync(hoseToolPart.Position, interactionPart.Position);

                local waypoints = path:GetWaypoints();
                if path.Status == Enum.PathStatus.Success then
                    local waypointCount = #waypoints;

                    local partCount = getPartCount(lastHosePart, 0);


                    if waypointCount > partCount then
                        waypointCount = waypointCount - partCount;

                        for i = 1, waypointCount do
                            local hosePart = workspace.HosePart:Clone();
                            hosePart.Parent = workspace;
                            hosePart.Position = lastHosePart.Position + (waypoints[i].Position - lastHosePart.Position).Unit * longestSide * i;
                            joinTwoParts(lastHosePart, hosePart);
                            hosePart.Anchored = false;
                            lastHosePart = hosePart;
                        end;
                        joinTwoParts(lastHosePart, hoseToolPart);
                    end;
                end;
            task.wait(0.1);
            end
        end)
    end) ]]
    
    NetworkService.Connect(ATTACH_ATTACK_LINE_EVENT, function(plr, interactionPart)
        if plr.Team.Name ~= 'Vancouver Fire & Rescue Service' then return; end;
        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= "Instance" then return; end;

        local attackLine = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Attack Line');
        if not attackLine then return; end;

        local waterCapacityValue = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
        waterCapacityValue.Name = 'WaterCapacity';
        waterCapacityValue.Parent = attackLine;
        waterCapacityValue.Value = interactionPart.Parent.Parent.Config.WaterCapacity;

        NetworkService.SendAll('FireHoseReplication', plr, interactionPart); --This tells clients to start replicating fire hose
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('FireHoseEnabled', function(plr)
        if not plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Attack Line') then return; end;

        plr.Character['Attack Line'].Emit.Water.Enabled = true;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('FireHoseDisabled', function(plr)
        if not plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Attack Line') then return; end;

        plr.Character['Attack Line'].Emit.Water.Enabled = false;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect(ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TRUCK_EVENT, function(plr, interactionPart)
        local supplyLine = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Supply Line');
        if not supplyLine then return; end;
        local truckButton = supplyLine.TruckButton;
        truckButton.Value = interactionPart;
        local fakeHose = interactionPart.fakeHose;
        supplyLine.Spring.Value = fakeHose
        fakeHose.Visible = true;
        fakeHose.Attachment1 = supplyLine.LineEnd:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment');
        setChildrenTransparency(supplyLine, 0)
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect(ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TANK_EVENT, function(plr, interactionPart)
        --for fire hydrant or a tank
        local supplyLine = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Supply Line');
        if not supplyLine then return; end;

        local truckButton = supplyLine.TruckButton;
        local hydrant = supplyLine.Hydrant
        hydrant.Value = interactionPart;
        local fakeHose = truckButton.Value.fakeHose;
        fakeHose.Attachment1 = interactionPart:FindFirstChildOfClass('Attachment');
        local truck = truckButton.Value.Parent.Parent;
        local waterDisplay = truck.Body.WaterDisplay;
        local truckConfig = truck.Config;
        local waterCapacity = truckConfig.WaterCapacity;
        setChildrenTransparency(supplyLine, 1)
        for i = waterCapacity.Value, 100, 0.025 do
            waterCapacity.Value += 0.025;
            updateWaterDisplay(waterDisplay)
            wait()
        end;
        fakeHose.Attachment1 = nil;

        truckButton.Value = nil;
        hydrant.Value = nil;
        supplyLine.Spring.Value = nil;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('DETACH_ATTACK_LINE', function(plr, tool)
        if not typeof(tool) == 'Instance' then return; end;

        if not (tool.Parent == plr.Character) and not (tool.Parent == plr.Backpack) then return; end;

        local waterCapacity = tool:FindFirstChild('WaterCapacity');
        if not waterCapacity then return; end;

        waterCapacity:Destroy();
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect(DESTROY_SPRING_CONNECTION_EVENT, function(plr, tool)
        local spring = tool:FindFirstChild('Spring');
        if not spring then return; end;

        local SpringConstraint = spring.Value;
        SpringConstraint.Attachment1 = nil;

        if tool.Name == 'Supply Line' then
            for i,v in next, tool:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('ObjectValue') then
                    v.Value = nil;
                end;
            end;
        else
            workspace.HoseStorage[plr.Name]:Destroy();
        end;
    end);
end;

function FireHoseService:Init()
    local services = self.Services
    NetworkService = services.NetworkService;
    local Constants = self.Shared.Constants.FireHose;
    EXTINGUISH_EVENT = Constants.EXTINGUISH_EVENT;
    SPRAY_EVENT = Constants.SPRAY_EVENT;
    ATTACH_ATTACK_LINE_EVENT = Constants.ATTACH_ATTACK_LINE_EVENT;
    ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TRUCK_EVENT = Constants.ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TRUCK_EVENT;
    ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TANK_EVENT = Constants.ATTACH_SUPPLY_LINE_TO_TANK_EVENT
    DESTROY_SPRING_CONNECTION_EVENT = Constants.DESTROY_SPRING_CONNECTION_EVENT
end

return FireHoseService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/FishingService.lua ---

--[[
    FishingService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")
-- Fishing Service
-- Khizzer
-- November 5, 2022


local FishingService = {}
local NetworkService;

local function quadraticBezier(t, p0, p1, p2)
    return (1 - t)^2 * p0 + 2 * (1 - t) * t * p1 + t^2 * p2
end

function FishingService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('FishingRodCast', function(plr: Player, castPos: Vector3)
        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(castPos) > 100 then _G.AeroError(plr, 'You cannot cast your fishing rod that far') return end;

        local fishingRod = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Fishing Rod');
        if not fishingRod then _G.AeroError(plr, 'You do not have a fishing rod equipped') return end;

        local topOfHandle = fishingRod.Handle.Position + Vector3.new(0, fishingRod.Handle.Size.Y / 2, 0);

        local part = Instance.new('Part');
        part.Size = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1);
        part.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball;
        part.Parent = workspace;

        local numberValue = Instance.new('NumberValue');
        numberValue.Name = 'FishingRodCast';
        numberValue.Parent = fishingRod;

        local connection;
        local midPoint = topOfHandle:Lerp(castPos, 0.5) + Vector3.new(0, 5, 0);

        --print(topOfHandle, midPoint, castPos);

        connection = numberValue.Changed:Connect(function(newValue)
            part.CFrame = CFrame.new(quadraticBezier(newValue, topOfHandle, midPoint , castPos))
        end);

        fishingRod:SetAttribute('Cast', true);
        plr:SetAttribute('FishingMinigame', true);

        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'FishingMinigame');

--[[         task.delay(math.random(5, 20), function()
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'FishingMinigame');
        end); ]]

        local tween = TweenService:Create(numberValue, TweenInfo.new(0.7), {Value = 1});
        tween:Play();
        tween.Completed:Once(function()
            connection:Disconnect();
            numberValue:Destroy();
            tween:Destroy();
            --part:Destroy();
        end)
    end)
end;
    
function FishingService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;


return FishingService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/FistService.lua ---

--[[
    FistService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local Teams = game:GetService("Teams")

-- Fist Service
-- Khizzer
-- February 23, 2024


local NetworkService;
local DamageCharacter;
local CombatService;

--Glass damage sounds
local BREAK_SOUND_ID = "rbxassetid://4757900430";
local DAMAGE_SOUND_ID = "rbxassetid://1921336902";

local FIST_GLASS_DAMAGE = 25;

local FistService = {}

local prisonLastDestroyed = 0;

function FistService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('FistHit', function(plr, hit: Part)
        if typeof(hit) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;
        if not hit:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;

        if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(hit.Position) > 5 then return; end;

        if hit:IsDescendantOf(plr.Character) then return; end;

        if hit.Name == 'BreakableGlass' then
            local health = hit:GetAttribute('Health') or 100;

            local newHealth = health - 25;
            hit:SetAttribute('Health', newHealth);

            if newHealth <= 0 then
                local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
                breakSound.SoundId = BREAK_SOUND_ID;
                breakSound.Volume = 0.6;
                breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
                breakSound.Parent = hit;
                hit:Destroy();
            else
                local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
                breakSound.SoundId = DAMAGE_SOUND_ID;
                breakSound.Volume = 0.6;
                breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
                breakSound.Parent = hit;
                breakSound:Destroy();
            end
            return;
        end;

        if hit.Name == 'ToiletHitbox' then
            if plr.Team.Name ~= 'Prisoner' and plr.Team.Name ~= 'Civilian' then return end
            -- 2 or more CSC in game
            local cscInGame = #Teams['Correctional Service Canada']:GetPlayers() > 1
            if tick() - prisonLastDestroyed < (if cscInGame then 600 else 1200) then return end
            local lastDestroyed = hit:GetAttribute('LastDestroyed') or 0;
            if tick() - lastDestroyed < (if cscInGame then 600 else 1800) then
                return;
            end;

            local health = hit:GetAttribute('Health') or 100;
            health -= 10;

            hit:SetAttribute('Health', health);

            if health <= 0 then
                local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
                breakSound.SoundId = DAMAGE_SOUND_ID; -- BREAK_SOUND_ID
                breakSound.Volume = 1;
                breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
                breakSound.Parent = hit;
                breakSound:Destroy();
                local toilet = hit.Parent;
                hit:SetAttribute('LastDestroyed', tick());
                prisonLastDestroyed = tick();
                toilet.Parent = nil;
                task.delay(120, function()
                    toilet.Parent = workspace;
                    hit:SetAttribute('Health', 100);
                end)
            else
                local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
                breakSound.SoundId = DAMAGE_SOUND_ID;
                breakSound.Volume = 1;
                breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
                breakSound.Parent = hit;
                breakSound:Destroy();
            end
            return;
        end

        local humanoid = hit.Parent:FindFirstChildWhichIsA('Humanoid');
        if not humanoid then return; end;
        DamageCharacter(hit.Parent, 10, plr);

        local targetPlr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(hit.Parent);
        if targetPlr then
            CombatService:SetCombat(targetPlr, 60);
            CombatService:SetCombat(plr, 60);
        end

        local sound = Instance.new('Sound');
        sound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://8646342913';
        sound.Parent = hit;
        sound.PlayOnRemove = true;

        sound:Destroy();
    end)
end;

function FistService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    DamageCharacter = self.Modules.DamageCharacter;
    CombatService = self.Services.CombatService;
end


return FistService

--[[
    FlashlightService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local FlashlightService = {Client = {}};

local NEON_MATERIAL = Enum.Material.Neon;
local SMOOTH_MATERIAL = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

function FlashlightService:Start()
    self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('Flashlight', function(plr)
        local flashlight = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Flashlight') or plr.Character:FindFirstChild('PS | Flashlight');
        if not flashlight then return; end;

        local light = flashlight.Light;
        local shouldBeEnabled = light.Material == SMOOTH_MATERIAL;

        light.Material = shouldBeEnabled and NEON_MATERIAL or SMOOTH_MATERIAL;
        light.SpotLight.Enabled = shouldBeEnabled;

        flashlight.Handle.Toggle:Play();
    end);
end;

function FlashlightService:Init()

end;

return FlashlightService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/GunService.lua ---

--[[
    GunService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Debris = game:GetService('Debris');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkService;

local BulletHolePart;

local newInstance = Instance.new;
local findFirstChild = workspace.FindFirstChild;
local findFirstChildOfClass = workspace.FindFirstChildOfClass;
local mathMax = math.max;
local SendAll;
local MoneyService;
local WhitelistedTeams;
local Raycast;

--local baseplate = workspace.BulletStorage.Tracers;

local bulletTracerPrefab = game:GetService('ServerStorage').Gun.BulletTracer;

local IMPACT_SOUNDS;
local BREAK_SOUND_ID = 'rbxassetid://4757900430';

local CombatService;

local DamageCharacter;

type bulletTable = {
    BarrelPos: any,
    Hit: any,
    Pos: any,
    Normal: any,
    MouseDirection: any,
    ClientHitPos: any,
}

local GunService = {Client = {}};

function GetPlayersWithinRadius(position: Vector3, radius: number)
    local players = {};
    for _, player in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
        if player.Character and player.Character.PrimaryPart and (player.Character.PrimaryPart.Position-position).Magnitude <= radius then
            players[#players+1] = player
        end
    end
    return players
end

function GunService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GunReload', function(plr)
        local char = plr.Character;
        local gun = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
        if not gun then return; end;
        if not findFirstChild(gun, 'GunConfig') then return; end;
        local reload = gun.Handle.Reload;

        local reserveAmmo = gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo');
        if reserveAmmo == 0 then return; end;
        local maxReserveAmmo = gun:GetAttribute('MaxReserveAmmo');

        local maxAmmo = gun:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo');
        local ammo = gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
        local ammoUsed = maxAmmo - ammo;

        --Magazine drop effect
        local magazine = gun:FindFirstChild('Magazine');
        if magazine then
            local fakeMagazine = magazine:Clone();
            magazine.Transparency = 1;
            fakeMagazine.CanCollide = true;
            fakeMagazine:ClearAllChildren();
            fakeMagazine.CFrame = magazine.CFrame;
            fakeMagazine.Massless = true;
            fakeMagazine.Parent = workspace;
            Debris:AddItem(fakeMagazine, 5);
            task.delay(0.8, function()
                magazine.Transparency = 0;
            end)
        end;

        char.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(gun.ReloadAnimation):Play(nil, nil, 0.5);

        reload:Play();

        reload.Ended:Wait();

        if gun:GetAttribute('Ammo') ~= ammo then return; end; -- If filled ammo while reloading then cancel reload.

        if reserveAmmo < maxAmmo then
           gun:SetAttribute('ReserveAmmo', 0);
           gun:SetAttribute('Ammo', mathMax(0, reserveAmmo));
        else
            gun:SetAttribute('ReserveAmmo', mathMax(0, reserveAmmo - ammoUsed));
            gun:SetAttribute('Ammo', maxAmmo);
        end
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('BulletEffect', function(plr, barrelPos, hit, pos, normal, direction)
        local char = plr.Character;
        local gun = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
        if not gun then return; end;
        local ammo = gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
        if ammo <= 0 then return; end;
        local barrel = findFirstChild(gun, 'Barrel');
        if not barrel then return; end;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('Gun', function(plr: Player, event, ...)
        if event == 'Shoot' then
            local char = plr.Character;
            local gun = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
            if not gun then return; end;
            local ammo = gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
            if ammo <= 0 then return; end;
            local barrel = findFirstChild(gun, 'Barrel');
            local damage = gun:GetAttribute('Damage');
            if not barrel then return; end;

            --local handle = gun.Handle;

            --local pos, hit,--[[ mouseOriginPos, mouseOriginLookVector,]] clientHitPos, barrelPos = ...;

            local gunConfig = require(findFirstChild(gun, 'GunConfig'));
            local shotCount = gunConfig.ShotCount or 1;
            local range = gunConfig.Range or 300;

            local hits = ...;

            if #hits > shotCount then
                return;
            end;

            CombatService:SetCombat(plr, 60);

            for _, bulletTable: bulletTable in hits do
                --destructure bulletTable
                local barrelPos, hit, pos, normal, direction, clientHitPos = bulletTable.BarrelPos, bulletTable.Hit, bulletTable.Pos, bulletTable.Normal, bulletTable.MouseDirection, bulletTable.ClientHitPos;

                if not barrelPos then return; end;
                if not pos then return; end;
                if not normal then return; end;
                if not direction then return; end;
                if not clientHitPos then return; end;

                if typeof(barrelPos) ~= 'Vector3' then return; end;
                if typeof(pos) ~= 'Vector3' then return; end;
                if typeof(normal) ~= 'Vector3' then return; end;
                if typeof(direction) ~= 'Vector3' then return; end;
                if typeof(clientHitPos) ~= 'Vector3' then return; end;

                if direction.Magnitude > gunConfig.Range then continue; end;
                if (barrelPos - plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 10 then return; end;

                if hit then
                    local hitPos = hit.Position;
                    if (hitPos - barrel.Position).Magnitude > range then
                        continue;
                    end;
                    if (hitPos - clientHitPos).Magnitude > 12 then
                        continue;
                    end;
                    --[[local direction = (hitPos - mouseOriginPos).Unit;
                    local dot = mouseOriginLookVector:Dot(direction);
                    if dot < 0.9 then
                        return;
                    end;]]
                end;

                if hit and hit.Parent then
                    if typeof(hit) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;
                    NetworkService.SendWithinRadius(hit.Position, 300, 'CreateBulletHoles', pos, barrelPos, direction, plr)
                    local hitName = hit.Name;
                    local humanoid = findFirstChildOfClass(hit.Parent, 'Humanoid');
                    if humanoid then
                        local targetPlr = game:GetService('Players'):GetPlayerFromCharacter(humanoid.Parent);
                        if targetPlr then CombatService:SetCombat(targetPlr, 60); end;
                        local headshot = damage * 2;
                        DamageCharacter(humanoid.Parent, ((hitName == 'Head') and headshot) or damage, plr);
--                        humanoid:TakeDamage((hitName == 'Head') and 75 or damage);
                    elseif hitName == 'Wheel' and hit.CanCollide and (WhitelistedTeams.GetLEOTeams()[plr.Team.Name] ~= nil) then
                        local health = hit.Health;
                        --local newHealth = mathMax(health.Value - damage, 0)
                       local newHealth = mathMax(health.Value - 50, 0)
                        health.Value = newHealth;
                        if newHealth == 0 then
                            hit.CanCollide = false;
                        end;
                    elseif hitName == 'BreakableGlass' then
                        local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
                        breakSound.SoundId = BREAK_SOUND_ID;
                        breakSound.Volume = 0.6;
                        breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
                        breakSound.Parent = hit;
                        hit:Destroy();
                    end;
--[[                     if hit:FindFirstAncestor('Cars') then
                        local body = hit:FindFirstAncestor('Body');
                        if body then
                            local config = body.Parent.Config;
                            local health = config.State.Health;
                            local newHealth = mathMax((health.Value - damage) * 0.1, 0);
                            health.Value = newHealth;
                        end;
                    end; ]]
                end;

                --[[ local attachment0 = barrel.Attachment;  --TRACERS FOR MAY THE 4TH DO NOT ENABLE AGAIN



                local attachment1 = newInstance('Attachment');
                attachment1.Parent = baseplate;
                attachment1.WorldPosition = pos;

                local bulletTracer = bulletTracerPrefab:Clone();
                bulletTracer.Attachment0 = attachment0;
                bulletTracer.Attachment1 = attachment1;

                if self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams.CheckLEO(plr) then
                    bulletTracer.Color = ColorSequence.new {
                        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)),
                        ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(36, 63, 238))
                    }
                end

                bulletTracer.Parent = barrel;

                Debris:AddItem(bulletTracer, 0.2);
                Debris:AddItem(attachment1, 0.2); ]]
            end;

            gun:SetAttribute('Ammo', mathMax(0, ammo - 1));

            SendAll('GunEffect', gun);
        elseif event == 'Flashlight' then
            local char = plr.Character;
            local gun = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
            if not gun then return; end;
            local flashlight = findFirstChild(gun, 'Flashlight');
            if not flashlight then return; end;
            flashlight.Light:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight').Enabled = not flashlight.Light:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight').Enabled;
            flashlight.Light.Material = flashlight.Light:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight').Enabled and Enum.Material.Neon or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
        end;


    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('REFILL_DEALER', function(plr)
        local char = plr.Character;
        local gun = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool');
        if (not gun) or (not gun:FindFirstChild('GunConfig')) then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'No gun found');
            return;
        end;

        local price = --[[gun:GetAttribute("RefillPrice") or]] 100
        if plr.Money.Value < price then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Not enough money');
            return;
        end;

        if
            (gun:GetAttribute('Ammo') == gun:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo'))
            and (gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo') == gun:GetAttribute('MaxReserveAmmo'))
        then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Ammo is full');
            return;
        end;

        gun:SetAttribute('ReserveAmmo', math.min(gun:GetAttribute('ReserveAmmo') + 10, gun:GetAttribute('MaxReserveAmmo')));
        gun:SetAttribute('Ammo', gun:GetAttribute('MaxAmmo'));

        MoneyService:SubtractMoney(plr, price);
    end)
end;

function GunService:Init()
    local BulletStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
    BulletStorage.Parent = workspace;

    IMPACT_SOUNDS = {
        [Enum.Material.Metal] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Metal;
        [Enum.Material.CorrodedMetal] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Metal;
        [Enum.Material.DiamondPlate] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Metal;
        [Enum.Material.Wood] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Wood;
        [Enum.Material.WoodPlanks] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Wood;
        [Enum.Material.Grass] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Grass;
        [Enum.Material.Granite] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Stone;
        [Enum.Material.Brick] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Stone;
        [Enum.Material.Sandstone] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Stone;
        [Enum.Material.Concrete] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Concrete;
        [Enum.Material.Asphalt] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Concrete;
        [Enum.Material.Ice] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Ice;
        [Enum.Material.Snow] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Ice;
        [Enum.Material.Sand] = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Sand;
        Default = self.ServerAssets.BulletSounds.Default;
    }

    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    SendAll = NetworkService.SendAll;
    BulletHolePart = self.ServerAssets.BulletHole;
    Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast;
    DamageCharacter = self.Modules.DamageCharacter;
    CombatService = self.Services.CombatService;
    MoneyService = self.Services.MoneyService;
    WhitelistedTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams;
end;

return GunService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/HandcuffService.lua ---

--[[
    HandcuffService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local PhysicsService = game:GetService('PhysicsService');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');


local NetworkService;

local HANDCUFF_EVENT;
local GRAB_EVENT;

local crimesModule;

local whitelistedTeams;
local ziptie_whitelist;

local PrisonService;
local NotificationService;
local RecordService;
local PlayerService;
local WarrantDataService;

local function PlayHandcuffSoundOnCharacter(char)
    local cuffSound = Instance.new('Sound');
    cuffSound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://2745044724';
    --cuffSound.Volume = 0.55;
    cuffSound.Parent = char.HumanoidRootPart;
    cuffSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
    cuffSound:Destroy();
end;

local DataService;
local CitationService;
local GetData, SetData;

local FAILED_DATA_LOAD_MSG = 'Error loading data, sorry! Try rejoining.';
local PROTECTED_TOOLS = {"Building Tools", "F3X", "Delete", "Placeable Identifier", "Fists"}; -- Prevent these tools from removal via frisk

local function GetPlayerData(plr, dataName)
    local suc, data = pcall(GetData, plr, dataName);
    if not suc then plr:Kick(FAILED_DATA_LOAD_MSG); return; end;
    return data;
end;

local HandcuffService = {DiedConnections = {}};

local CAN_ARREST_CAF = {'CFNIS', '1MPR'}

function HandcuffService:Start()
    local parts = 'Head Left Right';

    local function grab(plr, suspectRootPart)
        local suspect = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);

        local suspectCharacter = suspectRootPart.Parent;
        local victimHumanoid = suspectCharacter.Humanoid;
        local victimRootPart = suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart;
        local plrRootPart = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart;

        --Need check if player and suspect aren't grabbed together
        if not plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
            --- makes them grab suspect
            if suspect:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= nil then return; end;

            if victimHumanoid.Sit then
                local seatPart = victimHumanoid.SeatPart;
                if seatPart then
                    if seatPart:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld') then
                        seatPart.SeatWeld:Destroy();
                        task.wait(1);
                    end;
                else
                    victimHumanoid.Jump = true;
                    task.wait(1);
                end;
            end;

            victimHumanoid:UnequipTools();
            victimHumanoid.JumpPower = 0;

            for _,v in suspect.Backpack:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    v.Parent = suspect;
                end;
            end;

            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -2);
            suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', plr.Name);
            suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', plr.Name);
            suspect:SetAttribute('InZipties', nil);
            local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
            weld.Parent = plr.Character.Torso;
            weld.Part0 = suspectCharacter.Torso;
            weld.Part1 = plr.Character.Torso;
            suspectCharacter.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true;
            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart:SetNetworkOwner(plr);
            plrRootPart.RootPriority = 55;

            for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                    v.Massless = true;
                    v.CanCollide = false;
                end;
                if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                    v.CollisionGroup = 'Character';
                end;
            end;

            suspect:SetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle', nil);
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', true);
            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SuspectCuffAnimation', false);
            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SuspectCuffAnimation', true);
            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart:SetNetworkOwner(plr);

            -- TODO: I have no clue if this should be here or what
            self.DiedConnections[plr] = plr.Character.Humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                pcall(function()
                    suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', nil);
                    suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);
                end);
                pcall(function()

                    if weld and weld.Parent then weld:Destroy(); end;
                    if victimHumanoid then
                        victimHumanoid.PlatformStand = false;
                        victimRootPart:SetNetworkOwnershipAuto();
                        for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                            if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                                v.Massless = false;
                                v.CanCollide = false;
                            end;
                            if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                                v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
                            end
                        end;
                    end;

                    --networkEvent:FireClient(suspect, 'Uncuffed');

                    for i, v in next, suspect:GetChildren() do
                        if v:IsA('Tool') then
                            v.Parent = suspect.Backpack;
                        end;
                    end;

                    local oldConnection = self.DiedConnections[plr];
                    oldConnection:Disconnect();
                    self.DiedConnections[plr] = nil;
                end);
            end)
        else
            --- removes grab weld
            if suspect:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') then
                suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);
                suspectCharacter.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false;
                suspectCharacter.Humanoid.JumpPower = 50
                suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart:SetNetworkOwner(suspect);
                plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy()
                for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                    if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                        v.Massless = false;
                        v.CanCollide = false;
                    end;
                    if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                        v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
                    end
                end;
                victimHumanoid.JumpPower = 50;
            end;

            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);
        end;
    end

    NetworkService.Connect(HANDCUFF_EVENT, function(plr, suspectRootPart)
        if not whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;

        local suspect = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
        if not suspect then return; end;

        local rootPart = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart;

        local humanoid = plr.Character.Humanoid;

        local suspectChar = suspect.Character;
        local suspectHumanoid = suspectChar.Humanoid;

        if (rootPart.Position - suspectRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

        if not suspect:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then
            if suspect.Team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' then
                if not table.find(CAN_ARREST_CAF, plr:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h') and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(plr) then return; end;
            else
                if whitelistedTeams[suspect.Team.Name] and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(plr) then return; end;
            end;

            PlayHandcuffSoundOnCharacter(suspectChar);

            suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', plr.Name);
            suspect:SetAttribute('InZipties', nil);

            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SetInventoryEnabled', false);
            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SuspectCuffAnimation', true);

            suspectHumanoid:UnequipTools();

            for _,v in suspect.Backpack:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    v.Parent = suspect;
                end;
            end;

            grab(plr, suspectRootPart)
        else
            local suspectCharacter = suspect.Character;
            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart:SetNetworkOwner(suspect);

            suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', nil);
            suspect:SetAttribute('InZipties', nil);
            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SetInventoryEnabled', true);

            local targetToolParent = suspect.Backpack;

            if suspect:GetAttribute('Ragdoll') then
                targetToolParent = PlayerService:GetPlayerSessionStorage(suspect).DeathToolStorage;
            end;

            for _,v in suspect:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    v.Parent = targetToolParent;
                end;
            end;

            suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);
            suspectCharacter.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false;

            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SuspectCuffAnimation', false);
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);

            if plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
                plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy();
            end;

            for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                    v.Massless = false;
                    v.CanCollide = false;
                end;
                if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                    v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
                end
            end;

            suspectHumanoid.JumpPower = 50;
            suspect:SetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle', nil);
        end;
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect(GRAB_EVENT, function(plr, suspectRootPart)
        if not whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;
        grab(plr, suspectRootPart)
    end);

    NetworkService.Connect('PlaceInVehicle', function(plr, seat, victimHumanoid)
        if not whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and not ziptie_whitelist[plr:GetAttribute("Division") or "h"] and not ziptie_whitelist[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;
        if seat.Name ~= 'Rear' then return; end;
        local char = plr.Character;
        if not char then return; end;
        local victim = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(victimHumanoid.Parent);
        if not victim then return; end;
        if not victim:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') then return; end;

        victim:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);

        victimHumanoid.PlatformStand = false;
        victimHumanoid.JumpPower = 0;
        victimHumanoid.WalkSpeed = 0;
        victimHumanoid.RootPart:SetNetworkOwner(victim);

        if plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
            plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy();
        end;

        for _,v in next, victimHumanoid.Parent:GetDescendants() do
            if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                v.Massless = false;
                v.CanCollide = false;
            end;
            if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
            end
        end;

        victim:SetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle', true);
        seat:Sit(victimHumanoid);
        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('bookPlayer', function(plr, suspect, crimes, description)
        if not whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] then return; end;
        if not suspect then return; end;
        local totalTime = 0;

        local grabbedBy = suspect:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy');
        if not grabbedBy then return; end;
        if grabbedBy ~= plr.Name then return; end;

        for _,v in next, crimes do
            for a,b in next, crimesModule do
                if v == a then
                totalTime += b
                end;
            end;
        end;

        if totalTime == 0 then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Error while booking player: prison time resolved to 0');
            return;
        end;

        if totalTime > 1800 then
            totalTime = 1800;
        end;

        suspect:SetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle', nil);

        local teamAbbreviation = plr.Team:GetAttribute('Abbreviation');
        if not teamAbbreviation then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Team abbreviation not found. Report to developer.');
        end;

        RecordService:AddArrest(plr.Name, teamAbbreviation, suspect, totalTime, crimes, description)
        CitationService.PendingCitations[plr] = nil;

		plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy();

        NetworkService.Send(plr, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);

        RecordService:RemoveBolo(suspect);
        suspect:SetAttribute("LifeStart", os.time());
        task.spawn(WarrantDataService.RemovePlayerWarrants, WarrantDataService, suspect);

        for _,v in next, suspect:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Tool') then
                v:Destroy();
            end;
        end;

        NotificationService.SendAll('Prison', `{suspect.Name} has been imprisoned for {math.floor(totalTime / 60)} minutes.`, nil, 'Black');
        PrisonService.AddPrisonerSignal:Fire(suspect, totalTime);
    end);

    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('Frisk', function(plr, victim)
        if not whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then return; end;

        local tbl = {};

        for _,v in victim:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Tool') then
                tbl[#tbl+1] = v;
            end;
        end;

        return tbl;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('RemoveTool', function(plr, victim, toolName)
        if not whitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name] and plr:GetAttribute('Division') ~= 'GCPS' then return; end;

        if not victim:FindFirstChild(toolName) then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Could not find a tool with that name in victim.');
            return;
        end;

        if victim[toolName]:GetAttribute("DoNotRemove") == true or table.find(PROTECTED_TOOLS, toolName) then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', "That tool can't be removed");
            return;
        end

        victim[toolName].Parent = plr.Backpack;
    end)
end;

function HandcuffService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    DataService = self.Modules.DataService;
    GetData = DataService.Get;
    SetData = DataService.Set;
    PrisonService = self.Services.PrisonService;
    NotificationService = self.Services.NotificationService;
    RecordService = self.Services.RecordService;
    crimesModule = require(game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild('CrimesModule'));
    PlayerService = self.Services.PlayerService;
    CitationService = self.Services.CitationService;
    WarrantDataService = self.Modules.WarrantDataService;

    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff;
    HANDCUFF_EVENT = constants.HANDCUFF_EVENT;
    GRAB_EVENT = constants.GRAB_EVENT

    whitelistedTeams = constants.WhitelistedTeams;
    ziptie_whitelist = self.Shared.Constants.Ziptie.Whitelist;

    PhysicsService:RegisterCollisionGroup('Parts');
    PhysicsService:RegisterCollisionGroup('Character');

    PhysicsService:CollisionGroupSetCollidable('Parts', 'Default', true);
    PhysicsService:CollisionGroupSetCollidable('Parts', 'Character', false); --Handcuffed people

    task.spawn(function()
        for _,v in workspace:GetDescendants() do
            if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                if v.CollisionGroup == 'Default' then
                    v.CollisionGroup = 'Parts';
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end)
end;

return HandcuffService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/MeleeWeaponService.lua ---

--[[
    MeleeWeaponService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
-- Melee Service
-- Khizzer
-- June 17, 2021

local BREAK_SOUND_ID = 'rbxassetid://4757900430';

local MeleeWeaponService = {Client = {}};

local DamageCharacter;

local CombatService;

function MeleeWeaponService:Start()
    self.Services.NetworkService.Connect('MeleeWeapon', function(plr, event, hit)
        if (plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - hit.Position).Magnitude > 8 then return; end;

        if not typeof(hit) == "Instance" then return; end;

        local weapon = plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool');
        if not weapon then return; end;

        if weapon:GetAttribute('Module') ~= 'MeleeWeapon' then return; end;

        if event == 'CharacterHit' then

            local baseDamage = weapon:GetAttribute('BaseDamage');
            local critDamage = weapon:GetAttribute('CritDamage');

            local swingSound =  weapon.Handle.Swing;
            swingSound:Play()

            if not baseDamage then return; end;
            if not critDamage then return; end;


            local humanoid = hit.Parent:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid');
            
            if not humanoid then return; end;

            DamageCharacter(humanoid.Parent, math.random(baseDamage - math.random(0, 10), baseDamage), plr);
            CombatService:SetCombat(Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(humanoid.Parent), 60);
            CombatService:SetCombat(plr, 60);

        elseif event == 'BreakableGlassHit' then
            if not weapon:GetAttribute('CanBreakWindows') then return; end;

            local breakSound = Instance.new('Sound');
            breakSound.SoundId = BREAK_SOUND_ID;
            breakSound.Volume = 0.6;
            breakSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
            breakSound.Parent = hit;

            hit:Destroy();
        end;
    end)
end;

function MeleeWeaponService:Init()
    DamageCharacter = self.Modules.DamageCharacter;
    CombatService = self.Services.CombatService;
end;


return MeleeWeaponService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/PepperGunService.lua ---

--[[
    PepperGunService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Debris = game:GetService('Debris');

local NetworkService;

local newInstance = Instance.new;
local findFirstChild = workspace.FindFirstChild;
local findFirstChildOfClass = workspace.FindFirstChildOfClass;
local mathMax = math.max;
local addItem = Debris.AddItem;

local baseplate = workspace.Baseplate;
local Players = game:GetService('Players')

local bulletTracerPrefab = game:GetService('ServerStorage').Gun.BulletTracer;

local SendAll;

local GunService = {Client = {}};

function GunService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('PepperGun', function(plr, event, ...)
        if event == 'Shoot' then
            local char = plr.Character;
            local gun = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
            if not gun then return; end;
            local ammo = gun:GetAttribute('Ammo');
            if ammo <= 0 then return; end;
            local barrel = findFirstChild(gun, 'Barrel');
            if not barrel then return; end;

            local pos, hit, clientHitPos = ...;
            
            if not typeof(hit) == "Instance" then return; end;
            if not typeof(pos) == "Vector3" then return; end;
            if not typeof(clientHitPos) == "Vector3" then return; end;


            if hit then
                local hitPos = hit.Position;
                if (hitPos - barrel.Position).Magnitude > 210 then
                    return;
                end;
                if (hitPos - clientHitPos).Magnitude > 12 then
                    return;
                end;
            end;

            gun:SetAttribute('Ammo', mathMax(0, ammo - 1));

            if hit then
                local hitName = hit.Name;
                local humanoid: Humanoid = findFirstChildOfClass(hit.Parent, 'Humanoid');
				if humanoid then
                    NetworkService.Send(Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(humanoid.Parent), 'PepperSpray')
                    humanoid.Sit = true;
                end;
            end;
            SendAll('GunEffect', gun);
        end;
    end);
end;

function GunService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    SendAll = NetworkService.SendAll;
end;

return GunService;
