--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/PepperSprayService.lua ---

--[[
    PepperSprayService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkService;

local PEPPER_SPRAY_EVENT = 'PepperSpray';

local Send;

local PepperSprayService = {Client = {}};

function PepperSprayService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('PepperSpray', function(plr, event, hit)
        local pepperSpray = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Pepper Spray')
            or plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild('Pepper Spray')
            or plr.Character:FindFirstChild('PS | Pepper Spray')
            or plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild('PS | Pepper Spray');
        if not pepperSpray then return; end;
        local nossle = pepperSpray.Nossle;

        if not typeof(hit) == "Instance" then return; end;

        if event == 'Spray' and nossle.Spray.Enabled then
            if (pepperSpray.Hitbox.Position - hit.Position).Magnitude > 5 then return; end;
            local hitChar = hit.Parent;
            Send(Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(hitChar), PEPPER_SPRAY_EVENT);
            hitChar.Humanoid.Sit = true;
        elseif event == 'Enable' then
            nossle.Spray.Enabled = true;
            nossle.SpraySound:Play();
            pepperSpray.AncestryChanged:Wait();
            nossle.Spray.Enabled = false;
            nossle.SpraySound:Stop();
        elseif event == 'Disable' then
            nossle.Spray.Enabled = false;
            nossle.SpraySound:Stop();
        end;
    end);
end;

function PepperSprayService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    Send = NetworkService.Send;
end;

return PepperSprayService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/PlaceableService.lua ---

--[[
    PlaceableService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

local NetworkService;

local PLACE_EVENT;
local PICK_UP_EVENT;
local MIN_DISTANCE_FROM_OTHER_PLACEABLE = 1;

local placeables = ReplicatedStorage.Placeables;
local RemoveWhitespace;

local placedCFrames = {};

local PlaceableService = {Client = {}};

function AddNumberAttribute(instance: Instance, name: string, limit: number)
	name = RemoveWhitespace(name);
	local currentNumber = instance:GetAttribute(name);
	if not currentNumber then
		instance:SetAttribute(name, 1);
	else
		if currentNumber <= (limit - 1) then
			instance:SetAttribute(name, currentNumber + 1);
		else
			return 'LimitReached'
		end;
	end;
end;

function SubtractNumberAttribute(instance: Instance, name: string)
	name = RemoveWhitespace(name);
	local currentNumber = instance:GetAttribute(name);
	if not currentNumber then
		return;
	else
		if currentNumber >= 2 then
			instance:SetAttribute(name, currentNumber - 1);
		else
			instance:SetAttribute(name, nil);
		end;
	end;
end;

function PlaceableService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect(PLACE_EVENT, function(plr, cframe)
		local char = plr.Character;

		local placeableTool = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool');
		if placeableTool:GetAttribute('Module') ~= 'Placeable' then return; end;

		if (char.HumanoidRootPart.Position - cframe.Position).Magnitude > 8 then return; end;

		local model = placeables[placeableTool:GetAttribute('Model')];
		local placeableConfig = require(model.PlaceableConfig)
		if
      not placeableConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name]
      and not placeableConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h']
    then
      if placeableConfig.Condition then
        if not placeableConfig.Condition(plr) then return end
      else
        return
      end
    end

		for i, v in next, placedCFrames do
			if (v == cframe) or ((cframe.Position - v.Position).Magnitude < MIN_DISTANCE_FROM_OTHER_PLACEABLE) then
				return;
			end;
		end;

		-- local limitReached = AddNumberAttribute(plr, model.Name..'Limit', 20);
		-- if limitReached == 'LimitReached' then
		--	NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Placeable limit for ' ..  model.Name .. ' reached')
		--	return;
		-- end;
		if model.Name == 'Spike Strip' then
			for _, x in workspace:GetChildren() do
				if x.Name == model.Name and x:GetAttribute('PlacedBy') == plr.Name then
					_G.AeroError(plr, `{model.Name} is unique; you can only place one at a time.`)
					return;
				end
			end
			NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Notification', 'CAUTION', `You can only place one {model.Name} at a time, make sure you remove this placeable.`, nil, 'Red');
		end
		local clone = model:Clone();
		local primaryPart = clone.PrimaryPart;
		clone:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(cframe);
		clone:SetAttribute('PlacedBy', plr.Name);
		CollectionService:AddTag(primaryPart, 'Placeable');
		placedCFrames[primaryPart] = cframe;
		clone.Parent = workspace;
	end);

	NetworkService.Connect(PICK_UP_EVENT, function(plr, primaryPart)
		if not primaryPart then return; end;
		if not typeof(primaryPart) == 'Instance' then return; end;

		if not primaryPart:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;
		if not primaryPart.Parent then return; end;
		local placeableConfig = require(primaryPart.Parent.PlaceableConfig)
		if
      not placeableConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr.Team.Name]
      and not placeableConfig.WhitelistedTeams[plr:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h']
    then
      if placeableConfig.Condition then
        if not placeableConfig.Condition(plr) then return end
      else
        return
      end
    end
		if (plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - primaryPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

		placedCFrames[primaryPart] = nil;
		-- local placedBy = primaryPart.Parent:GetAttribute('PlacedBy');
		-- if placedBy then
		-- 	if game.Players:FindFirstChild(placedBy) then
		-- 		SubtractNumberAttribute(game.Players:FindFirstChild(placedBy), primaryPart.Parent.Name..'Limit', 0)
		-- 	end;
		-- end;

		primaryPart.Parent:Destroy();
	end);
end;

function PlaceableService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;

	local constants = self.Shared.Constants.Placeable;
	PLACE_EVENT = constants.PLACE_EVENT;
	PICK_UP_EVENT = constants.PICK_UP_EVENT;
	RemoveWhitespace = self.Shared.StringUtil.RemoveWhitespace
end;

return PlaceableService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/ProtestSignService.lua ---

--[[
    ProtestSignService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Protest Sign Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 22, 2022



local ProtestSignService = {};
local NetworkService;
local FilterStringAsync;

function ProtestSignService:Start()
    CooldownService:Create('ProtestSignCustomisation');

    NetworkService.Connect('PROTEST_SIGN_CUSTOMISATION', function(plr, colour, font, text)
        if CooldownService:Check('ProtestSignCustomisation', plr) then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Please wait a few seconds before trying again.');
            return;
        end;

        local protestSign = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Protest Sign');
        
        if not protestSign then return; end;

        local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(text, plr.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);
        if not filterResult then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        local filteredText = filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();

        CooldownService:Add('ProtestSignCustomisation', plr, 2);

        if not filteredText then
            NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        local signGUI = protestSign.Sign.SignGUI;
        local background = signGUI.Background;
        local textLabel: TextLabel = background.TextLabel;

        background.BackgroundColor3 = colour;
        textLabel.Font = Enum.Font[font];
        textLabel.Text = filteredText;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('PROTEST_SIGN_SOUND', function(plr)
        local protestSign = plr.Character:FindFirstChild('Protest Sign');
        
        if not protestSign then return; end;
        if protestSign:GetAttribute('Cooldown') then return; end;

        local sounds = protestSign.Handle:GetChildren();

        local chosenSound = sounds[math.random(1,3)];
        chosenSound:Play();

        task.defer(function()
            protestSign:SetAttribute('Cooldown', true);
            task.wait(1);
            protestSign:SetAttribute('Cooldown', nil);
        end)
    end)
end;

function ProtestSignService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    local Filter = self.Modules.Filter;
    FilterStringAsync = Filter.FilterStringAsync;
    CooldownService = self.Shared.CooldownService;
end;


return ProtestSignService

--[[
    RepairCarService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Repair Car Service
-- Khizzer
-- September 6, 2021



local RepairCarService = {}

local REPAIR_CAR_EVENT = 'RepairCar'

local NetworkService;


function RepairCarService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect(REPAIR_CAR_EVENT, function(plr, car)
        if not car:FindFirstChild('Chassis') then return; end;
        local repairing = true;
        local platform = car.Chassis.Platform;
        
        platform:SetAttribute('BeingRepaired', true);
        
        coroutine.wrap(function()
            local char = plr.Character;
            local rootPart = char.HumanoidRootPart;
            while repairing and ((rootPart.Position - platform.Position).Magnitude <= 10) and char:FindFirstChild('Repair Tool') do
                task.wait();
            end;
            if repairing then
                repairing = false;
                platform:SetAttribute('BeingRepaired', nil);
                NetworkService.Send(plr, REPAIR_CAR_EVENT, 'Cancelled');
            end;
        end)();

        for i = 10, 0, -1 do
            if not repairing then break; end;
            NetworkService.Send(plr, REPAIR_CAR_EVENT, i);
            if i == 0 then break; end;
            task.wait(1);
        end;

        if repairing then
            platform:SetAttribute('BeingRepaired', nil);
            car.Config.State.Health.Value = 100;
        end;
    end)
end;


function RepairCarService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;


return RepairCarService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/RiotShieldService.lua ---

--[[
    RiotShieldService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local RiotShieldService = {}

local NetworkService;

function RiotShieldService:_weldShield(shield: Model, character: Model)
    local handle = shield.Handle;
    for i, v in next, shield:GetDescendants() do
        if (v:IsA('BasePart') or v:IsA('Seat')) and not v:GetAttribute('NoWeld') then
            local weld = Instance.new('Weld');
            weld.Part0 = v;
            weld.Part1 = handle;
            weld.C0 = v.CFrame:Inverse() * handle.CFrame;
            weld.Parent = v;
            v.Anchored = false;
        end;
    end;

    local c0 = shield:GetAttribute('C0');
    local c1 = shield:GetAttribute('C1');

    local leftArm = character['Left Arm'];

    local leftArmWeld = Instance.new('Weld');
    leftArmWeld.Part0 = leftArm;
    leftArmWeld.Part1 = handle;
    leftArmWeld.C0 = c0;
    leftArmWeld.C1 = c1;
    leftArmWeld.Parent = handle;
end

function RiotShieldService:Start()
    local SHIELD_HOLD_ANIM = self.ServerAssets.Shields.ShieldHoldAnim;

    NetworkService.Connect('RIOT_SHIELD', function(plr: Player)
        local character = plr.Character;
        if not character then return end;

        local animator = character.Humanoid:FindFirstChildOfClass('Animator');

        if character:FindFirstChild('RIOT_SHIELD') then
            character.ShieldHoldAnim:Destroy();
            for _,v in animator:GetPlayingAnimationTracks() do
                if v.Name == 'RiotShieldAnimation' then
                    v:Stop();
                end;
            end;
            character:FindFirstChild('RIOT_SHIELD'):Destroy();
            return;
        end;

        local shield = character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Tool');
        if not shield then return end;

        if not shield:GetAttribute('Module') == 'RiotShield' then return; end;

        local shieldModel = self.ServerAssets.Shields:FindFirstChild(shield.Name);
        if not shieldModel then return end;

        local shieldClone = shieldModel:Clone();
        shieldClone.Parent = character;
        shieldClone.Name = 'RIOT_SHIELD';

        local animation = SHIELD_HOLD_ANIM:Clone();
        animation.Parent = character;

        local track = animator:LoadAnimation(animation);
        track.Name = 'RiotShieldAnimation';
        track.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action4;
        track.Looped = true;
        track:Play();

        self:_weldShield(shieldClone, character);
    end)
end;

function RiotShieldService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return RiotShieldService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/TaserService.lua ---

--[[
    TaserService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local NetworkService;

local mathMax = math.max;
local findFirstChild = workspace.FindFirstChild;
local findFirstChildOfClass = workspace.FindFirstChildOfClass;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;

local function PlayTaseSoundOnCharacter(char)
    local taseSound = Instance.new('Sound');
    taseSound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://277635663';
    taseSound.Volume = 0.55;
    taseSound.Parent = char.HumanoidRootPart;
    taseSound:Play();
    return taseSound;
end;

local TaserService = {Client = {}};

function GetPlayersWithinRadius(position: Vector3, radius: number)
    local players = {};
    for _, player in ipairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
        if player.Character and player.Character.PrimaryPart and (player.Character.PrimaryPart.Position-position).Magnitude <= radius then
            players[#players+1] = player
        end
    end
    return players
end

function TaserService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('TaserReload', function(plr)
        local char = plr.Character;
        local taser = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
        if not taser then return; end;
        if not findFirstChild(taser, 'TaserConfig') then return; end;
        local reload = taser.Handle.Reload;

        local reserveAmmo = taser:GetAttribute('ReserveCartridges');
        if reserveAmmo == 0 then return; end;

        local maxCartridges = taser:GetAttribute('MaxCartridges');
        local cartridges = taser:GetAttribute('Cartridges');
        local cartridgesUsed = maxCartridges - cartridges;

        char.Humanoid.Animator:LoadAnimation(taser.ReloadAnimation):Play(nil, nil, 0.5);

        reload:Play();
        reload.Ended:Wait();

        if taser:GetAttribute('Cartridges') ~= cartridges then return; end; -- If replaced cartridge while reloading then cancel reload.

        taser.Cartridge.Transparency = 0;

        taser:SetAttribute('ReserveCartridges', mathMax(0, reserveAmmo - cartridgesUsed));
        taser:SetAttribute('Cartridges', maxCartridges);
    end)


    NetworkService.Connect('Taser', function(plr, event, ...)
        if event == 'Shoot' then
            local char = plr.Character;
            local taser = findFirstChildOfClass(char, 'Tool');
            if not taser then return; end;
            local cartridges = taser:GetAttribute('Cartridges');
            if cartridges <= 0 then return; end;
            local barrel = findFirstChild(taser, 'Barrel');
            if not barrel then return; end;

            local --[[pos,]] hit, clientHitPos = ...;

            if hit then
                local hitPos = hit.Position;
                if (hitPos - barrel.Position).Magnitude > 21.5 then
                    -- print('hitPos is too far from barrel. Check failed');
                    return;
                end;
                if (hitPos - clientHitPos).Magnitude > 18 then
                    -- print('hitPos is too far from clientHitPos. Check failed');
                    return;
                end;
            end;

            taser:SetAttribute('Cartridges', mathMax(0, cartridges - 1));

            if hit then
                local targetChar = hit.Parent;
                local humanoid = findFirstChildOfClass(targetChar, 'Humanoid');
                if humanoid then
                    local targetPlr = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(targetChar);
                    coroutineWrap(function()
                        for _,v in next, GetPlayersWithinRadius(plr.Character.PrimaryPart.Position, 250) do
                            NetworkService.Send(v, 'TaserEffect', plr.Character['X-26'], targetChar.Torso)
                        end
                        local taseSound = PlayTaseSoundOnCharacter(targetChar);
                        NetworkService.Send(targetPlr, 'SetInventoryEnabled', false);
                        humanoid:UnequipTools();
                        humanoid.PlatformStand = true;
                        task.wait(4);
                        taseSound:Stop();
                        taseSound:Destroy();
                        humanoid.PlatformStand = if targetPlr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then true else false;
                        NetworkService.Send(targetPlr, 'SetInventoryEnabled', if targetPlr:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then false else true);
                    end)();
                end;
            end;

            taser.Cartridge.Transparency = 1;
            taser.Barrel.Light.Enabled = true;
            barrel.Shoot:Play();
            task.wait(0.13);
            taser.Barrel.Light.Enabled = false;
        end;
    end);
end;

function TaserService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return TaserService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/TirePumpService.lua ---

--[[
    TirePumpService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local NetworkService;

local TIRE_PUMP_EVENT = 'TirePump';

local wait;
local newInstance = Instance.new;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;

local Send;

local TirePumpService = {Client = {}};

function TirePumpService:Start()
	NetworkService.Connect(TIRE_PUMP_EVENT, function(plr, wheel)
        if not typeof(wheel) == 'Instance' then return; end;
        if not wheel:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;

        if (wheel.Name ~= 'Wheel') or (wheel.CanCollide) then return; end;
        local pumping = true;
        local isBeingPumped = newInstance('BoolValue');
        isBeingPumped.Name = 'IsBeingPumped';
        isBeingPumped.Parent = wheel;
		coroutineWrap(function()
			local char = plr.Character;
            local rootPart = char.HumanoidRootPart;
            while pumping and ((rootPart.Position - wheel.Position).Magnitude <= 6) and char:FindFirstChild('Tire Pump') do
                task.wait();
            end;
            if pumping then
                pumping = false;
                isBeingPumped:Destroy();
                isBeingPumped = nil;
                Send(plr, TIRE_PUMP_EVENT, 'Cancelled');
            end;
        end)();
        for i = 5, 0, -1 do
            if not pumping then break; end;
            Send(plr, TIRE_PUMP_EVENT, i);
            if i == 0 then break; end;
            wait(1);
        end;
        if pumping then
            wheel.CanCollide = true;
            wheel.Health.Value = 100;
            pumping = false;
            isBeingPumped:Destroy();
            isBeingPumped = nil;
        end;
    end);
end;

function TirePumpService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
    Send = NetworkService.Send;
end;

return TirePumpService;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/Tools/ZiptieService.lua ---

--[[
    ZiptieService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → Tools
    Parent: Tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Ziptie Service
-- Khizzer
-- November 9, 2023

local Players = game:GetService("Players")


local NetworkService: NetworkService
local PlayerService;
local WhitelistedTeams: {string: boolean};
local leo_whitelist;

local parts = 'Head Left Right';

local ZiptieService = {}
local DiedConnections = {}

local function PlayZiptieSoundOnCharacter(char)
    local cuffSound = Instance.new('Sound');
    cuffSound.SoundId = 'rbxassetid://15449290275';
    --cuffSound.Volume = 0.55;
    cuffSound.Parent = char.HumanoidRootPart;
    cuffSound.PlayOnRemove = true;
    cuffSound:Destroy();
end;

function ZiptieService:Start()
    local function grab(officer: Player, suspectRootPart: BasePart)
        if typeof(suspectRootPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;
        if not suspectRootPart:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;

        local officerCharacter = officer.Character;
        if not officerCharacter:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;

        local officerTeam = officer.Team.Name;
        local officerDivision = officer:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h';

        if not WhitelistedTeams[officerTeam] and not WhitelistedTeams[officerDivision] then return; end;

        local suspect: Player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
        if not suspect then return; end;

        local officerHumanoid: Humanoid = officerCharacter.Humanoid;
        local officerRootPart = officerHumanoid.RootPart;

        local suspectCharacter = suspect.Character;
        local suspectHumanoid: Humanoid = suspectCharacter.Humanoid;

        if (officerRootPart.Position - suspectRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;
        if officer.Team.Name == "Civilian" and officer:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" and not suspect:GetAttribute('InZipties') then return; end;
        if officer.Team.Name ~= "Civilian" or officer:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" then
            suspect:SetAttribute("InZipties", nil)
        end

        if not officerCharacter.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
            if suspect:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') ~= nil then return; end;

            if suspectHumanoid.Sit then
                local seatPart = suspectHumanoid.SeatPart;
                if seatPart then
                    if seatPart:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld') then
                        seatPart.SeatWeld:Destroy();
                        task.wait(1);
                    end;
                else
                    suspectHumanoid.Jump = true;
                    task.wait(1);
                end;
            end;

            suspectHumanoid:UnequipTools()
            suspectHumanoid.JumpPower = 0;

            for _,v in suspect.Backpack:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    v.Parent = suspect;
                end;
            end;

            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = officerRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -2);
            suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', officer.Name);
            suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', officer.Name);
            local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
            weld.Parent = officerCharacter.Torso;
            weld.Part0 = suspectCharacter.Torso;
            weld.Part1 = officerCharacter.Torso;
            suspectCharacter.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true;
            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart:SetNetworkOwner(officer);
            suspectRootPart.RootPriority = 55;

            for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                    v.Massless = true;
                    v.CanCollide = false;
                end;
                if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                    v.CollisionGroup = 'Character';
                end;
            end;

            suspect:SetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle', nil);
            NetworkService.Send(officer, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', true);
        else
            --Remove grab
            if not suspect:GetAttribute('GrabbedBy') then return end;
            suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);

            suspectCharacter.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false;
            suspectCharacter.Humanoid.JumpPower = 50
            suspectCharacter.HumanoidRootPart:SetNetworkOwner(suspect);
            officerCharacter.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy()
            for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                    v.Massless = false;
                    v.CanCollide = false;
                end;
                if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                    v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
                end
            end;
            suspectHumanoid.JumpPower = 50;

            NetworkService.Send(officer, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);
        end;
    end

    NetworkService.Connect('ZiptieRestrain', function(officer: Player, suspectRootPart: BasePart)
        if typeof(suspectRootPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;
        if not suspectRootPart:IsA('BasePart') then return; end;

        local officerCharacter = officer.Character;
        if not officerCharacter:FindFirstChild('Zipcuffs') then return; end;

        local officerTeam = officer.Team.Name;
        local officerDivision = officer:GetAttribute('Division') or 'h';

        if not WhitelistedTeams[officerTeam] and not WhitelistedTeams[officerDivision] then return; end;

        local suspect: Player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(suspectRootPart.Parent);
        if not suspect then return; end;

        local officerHumanoid: Humanoid = officerCharacter.Humanoid;
        local officerRootPart = officerHumanoid.RootPart;

        local suspectCharacter = suspect.Character;
        local suspectHumanoid: Humanoid = suspectCharacter.Humanoid;

        if (officerRootPart.Position - suspectRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 7 then return; end;

        if not suspect:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then
            if leo_whitelist[suspect.Team.Name] and officerDivision ~= "GCPS" and not _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(officer) then return; end;

            PlayZiptieSoundOnCharacter(suspectCharacter);

            suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', officer.Name);
            if officer.Team.Name == "Civilian" then
                suspect:SetAttribute('InZipties', true);
            end

            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SetInventoryEnabled', false);
            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SuspectCuffAnimation', true);

            suspectHumanoid:UnequipTools();

            for _,v in suspect.Backpack:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    v.Parent = suspect;
                end;
            end;

            grab(officer, suspectRootPart)
        else
            if officer.Team.Name == "Civilian" and officer:GetAttribute("Division") ~= "GCPS" and not suspect:GetAttribute('InZipties') then return; end;
            suspect:SetAttribute('HandcuffedBy', nil);
            suspect:SetAttribute('InZipties', nil);
            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SetInventoryEnabled', true);

            local targetToolParent = suspect.Backpack;

            if suspect:GetAttribute('Ragdoll') then
                targetToolParent = PlayerService:GetPlayerSessionStorage(suspect).DeathToolStorage;
            end;

            for _,v in suspect:GetChildren() do
                if v:IsA('Tool') then
                    v.Parent = targetToolParent;
                end;
            end;

            suspect:SetAttribute('GrabbedBy', nil);
            suspectHumanoid.PlatformStand = false;

            NetworkService.Send(suspect, 'SuspectCuffAnimation', false);
            NetworkService.Send(officer, 'OfficerCuffAnimation', false);

            if officerCharacter.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
                officerCharacter.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy();
                for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                    if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                        v.Massless = false;
                        v.CanCollide = false;
                    end;
                end;
            end;

            for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
                if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                    v.Massless = false;
                    v.CanCollide = false;
                end;
                if v:IsA('BasePart') then
                    v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
                end
            end;

            suspectHumanoid.JumpPower = 50;
            suspect:SetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle', nil);
        end;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('ZiptieGrab', function(officer: Player, suspectRootPart: BasePart)
        grab(officer, suspectRootPart)
    end)
end

function ZiptieService:Init()
    PlayerService = self.Services.PlayerService;
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    local ziptieConstants = self.Shared.Constants.Ziptie;
    WhitelistedTeams = ziptieConstants.Whitelist;
    leo_whitelist = self.Shared.Constants.Handcuff.WhitelistedTeams;
end

return ZiptieService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/ToolService.lua ---

--[[
    ToolService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Tool Service
-- Khizzer
-- February 25, 2023

local ServerStorage = game:GetService('ServerStorage');

local ToolService = {Client = {}}

local ProfileDataService;

function ToolService:LoadCivilianTools(plr: Player)
    local civilianToolData = ProfileDataService.GetData(plr, 'CivilianTools');
    for _,v in next, civilianToolData do
        local attributes = v.Attributes;
        local name = v.Name;

        local tool = ServerStorage:FindFirstChild(name);
        if tool and tool.Name ~= "Phone" then
            local newTool = tool:Clone();
            newTool:SetAttribute('DoNotSave', nil);
            newTool.Parent = plr.Backpack;
            for attrName, attrValue in next, attributes do
                newTool:SetAttribute(attrName, attrValue);
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

function ToolService:SaveCivilianTools(plr: Player)
    local character = plr.Character;
    if character then
        local humanoid = plr.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid');

        if humanoid then
            humanoid:UnequipTools();
        end;
    end

    local toolsToSave = {}

    for _,v in next, plr.Backpack:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Tool') then
            if v:GetAttribute('DoNotSave') then continue; end;
            if v.Name == "Phone" then continue end
            table.insert(toolsToSave, {
                Name = v.Name;
                Attributes = v:GetAttributes();
            })
        end;
    end;

    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'CivilianTools', toolsToSave);
end;

function ToolService:ResetSavedCivilianTools(plr)
    ProfileDataService.SetData(plr, 'CivilianTools', {});
end;

function ToolService:Start()

end


function ToolService:Init()
	ProfileDataService = self.Modules.ProfileDataService;
end


return ToolService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/TowTrucks/FlatbedService.lua ---

--[[
    FlatbedService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → TowTrucks
    Parent: TowTrucks
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
-- Tow Truck Service
-- Khizzer
-- January 14, 2023

local animating: {[Part]: boolean} = {};
local winchingIn = {};

local TowTruckService = {Client = {}, Connections = {}}

local EMPTY_VECTOR3 = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);

local NetworkService;
local Signal;
local GetPlayersWithinRadius;

local FirstAnimationSignal;
local FinalAnimationSignal;

local WinchStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
WinchStorage.Parent = workspace;
WinchStorage.Name = 'WinchStorage';

local BCAA_TEAM: Team = game.Teams['British Columbia Automobile Association'];

local WINCH_PREFAB: Tool? = nil;

function TowTruckService:_isNotStationary(plr: Player, truck: Model)
	local chassis: Model = truck.Chassis;
	local platform: Part = chassis.Platform;

	local platformVelocity: Vector3 = platform.AssemblyLinearVelocity;

	local platformVelocityMagnitude: number = platformVelocity.Magnitude;

	return platformVelocityMagnitude > 2
end

function TowTruckService:_lowerBed(truck: Model)
    local chassis: Model = truck.Chassis;
	local body: Model = truck.Body;

	local bed: Model = body.Bed;

	local platform: Part = chassis.Platform;
	local bedWeld: Weld = platform.BedWeld;

	local towTruckControls = body.Compartment.Controls;
	if towTruckControls:GetAttribute('Lowered') then return; end;
	if towTruckControls:GetAttribute('Moving') then return; end;

	local firstLoweredC0: CFrame? = bed:GetAttribute('FirstLoweredC0');
	local finalLoweredC0: CFrame? = bed:GetAttribute('FinalLoweredC0');

	local main: Part = bed.Main;

	platform.Anchored = true;
	platform.AssemblyLinearVelocity = EMPTY_VECTOR3;
	platform.AssemblyAngularVelocity = EMPTY_VECTOR3;

	local initial = bedWeld.C0;
	local startTime = tick();
	local steppedConnection;

	animating[main] = true;

	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Moving', true);
	steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
		local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3.5;
		if percent > 1 then
			steppedConnection:Disconnect();
			bedWeld.C0 = firstLoweredC0;
			FirstAnimationSignal:Fire();
			return;
		end;
		bedWeld.C0 = initial:Lerp(firstLoweredC0, percent);
	end);

	FirstAnimationSignal:Wait();
	steppedConnection:Disconnect();
	startTime = tick();
	steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
		local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3.5;
		if percent > 1 then
			steppedConnection:Disconnect();
			bedWeld.C0 = finalLoweredC0;
			FinalAnimationSignal:Fire();
			return;
		end;
		bedWeld.C0 = firstLoweredC0:Lerp(finalLoweredC0, percent);
	end);

	FinalAnimationSignal:Wait();
	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Moving', nil);
	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Raised', nil);
	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Lowered', true);
	main.CollisionGroup = 'Default';
	animating[main] = nil;
end;

function TowTruckService:_raiseBed(truck: Model)
	local chassis: Model = truck.Chassis;
	local body: Model = truck.Body;

	local bed: Model = body.Bed;

	local platform: Part = chassis.Platform;
	local bedWeld: Weld = platform.BedWeld;

	local towTruckControls = body.Compartment.Controls;
	if towTruckControls:GetAttribute('Raised') then return; end;
	if towTruckControls:GetAttribute('Moving') then return; end;

	local firstLoweredC0: CFrame? = bed:GetAttribute('FirstLoweredC0');

	local raisedC0 = CFrame.new();

	local main: Part = bed.Main;

	if animating[main] then return; end;

	main.CollisionGroup = 'CarBody';

	local initial = bedWeld.C0;
	local startTime = tick();
	local steppedConnection;

	animating[main] = true;

	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Moving', true);
	steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
		local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3.5;
		if percent > 1 then
			steppedConnection:Disconnect();
			bedWeld.C0 = firstLoweredC0;
			FirstAnimationSignal:Fire();
			return;
		end;
		bedWeld.C0 = initial:Lerp(firstLoweredC0, percent);
	end);

	FirstAnimationSignal:Wait();
	steppedConnection:Disconnect();

	startTime = tick();

	steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
		local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3.5;
		if percent > 1 then
			steppedConnection:Disconnect();
			bedWeld.C0 = raisedC0;
			FinalAnimationSignal:Fire();
			return;
		end;
		bedWeld.C0 = firstLoweredC0:Lerp(raisedC0, percent);
	end);
	FinalAnimationSignal:Wait();
	steppedConnection:Disconnect();
	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Moving', nil);
	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Lowered', nil);
	towTruckControls:SetAttribute('Raised', true);
	platform.Anchored = false;
	animating[main] = nil;
end;

function TowTruckService:_createWinch(plr: Player, bedWinchPart: Part)
	if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

	local char = plr.Character;
	local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid');

	if char:FindFirstChild('Winch') then return; end;

	local bedWinchPos = bedWinchPart.Position;

	local winch = WINCH_PREFAB:Clone();
	winch.Parent = plr.Backpack;

	if not humanoid then return; end;

	humanoid:UnequipTools();
	humanoid:EquipTool(winch);

	local plrsToReplicate: {Player} = GetPlayersWithinRadius(bedWinchPos, 100);
	for _, plrToReplicate in plrsToReplicate do
		NetworkService.Send(plrToReplicate, 'TowTruckWinch', {
			Player = plr;
			WinchTool = winch;
			BedPart = bedWinchPart;
		});
	end;

	-- self.Connections[plr] = winch.Handle:GetPropertyChangedSignal('CFrame'):Connect(function()
	-- 	local attachment0Pos = GetAttachmentWorldPosition(rope.Attachemnt0);
	-- 	local attachment1Pos = GetAttachmentWorldPosition(rope.Attachment1);

	-- 	local distanceBetweenAttachments = (attachment0Pos - attachment1Pos);
	-- 	local distanceBetweenAttachmentsMagnitude = distanceBetweenAttachments.Magnitude;
	-- 	print('CFrame changed');

	-- 	print(distanceBetweenAttachmentsMagnitude);

	-- 	rope.Length = distanceBetweenAttachmentsMagnitude + 2.5;

--[[ 		if rope.CurrentDistance >= rope.Length - 2 then
			print('Increasing rope');
			rope.Length = rope.CurrentLength + 2;
		elseif rope.CurrentDistance <= rope.Length - 3 then
			rope.Length = rope.CurrentLength - 2;
		end; ]]
--	end);
end;

function TowTruckService:_deletwWinch(plr: Player)
	if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

	local char = plr.Character;
	local humanoid = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Humanoid');

	humanoid:UnequipTools();

	local plrWinchPart = WinchStorage:FindFirstChild(plr.Name);

	if plrWinchPart then
		plrWinchPart:Destroy();
	end;

	local plrWinchConnection = self.Connections[plr];
	if plrWinchConnection then
		plrWinchConnection:Disconnect();
		self.Connections[plr] = nil;
	end;
end;


function TowTruckService:Start()
	FirstAnimationSignal = Signal.new();
	FinalAnimationSignal = Signal.new();

	NetworkService.Connect('_lowerTowTruckBed', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local car = plr.Car.Value;
		if not car then return; end;
		if not car.Body:FindFirstChild('Bed') then return; end;

		self:_lowerBed(car);
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('_raiseTowTruckBed', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local car = plr.Car.Value;
		if not car then return; end;
		if not car.Body:FindFirstChild('Bed') then return; end;

		self:_raiseBed(car);
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('_getFlatbedWinch', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local car = plr.Car.Value;
		if not car then return; end;
		if not car.Body:FindFirstChild('Bed') then return; end;

		local bedWinchPart = car.Body.Bed.Winch.WinchPart;
		
		self:_createWinch(plr, bedWinchPart);
	end)

	local function GetCar(child: Instance): Model
		if child.Parent == game then return; end;
		if child.Parent == workspace.Cars then
			return child;
		else
			return GetCar(child.Parent);
		end;
	end;

	NetworkService.Connect('_attachTow', function(plr: Player, towPart: Part)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local car: Model? = plr.Car.Value;
		if not car then return; end;

		local rope: RopeConstraint? = car.Body:FindFirstChild('WinchRope', true);
		if not rope then return; end;

		if self:_isNotStationary(plr, car) then return; end;

		local targetCar = GetCar(towPart);
		if not targetCar then return; end;

		local targetChassis = targetCar:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
		local targetPlatform = targetChassis.Platform;

		local towTruckPlatform = car.Chassis.Platform;

		if (targetPlatform.Position - towTruckPlatform.Position).Magnitude > 200 then
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'The car is too far away from the bed to tow');
			return;
		end;

		targetChassis.Mass.Massless = true;
		targetCar.Config.State.Hazards.Value = true;

		local attached = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
		attached.Name = 'Attached';
		attached.Value = towPart;
		attached.Parent = car.Body.Bed;

		targetCar:SetAttribute('BeingTowed');

		local originalOwner;

		for _,v in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
			if v.Car.Value == targetCar then
				originalOwner = v;
				v.Car.Value = nil;
				break;
			end;
		end;

		if originalOwner then
			if originalOwner.Car.Value == targetCar then
				local original = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
				original.Name = 'OriginalOwner';
				original.Value = originalOwner;
				original.Parent = targetCar;
			end;
		end;

		local attachment = Instance.new('Attachment');
		attachment.Parent = targetPlatform;
		attachment.Position = targetPlatform.CFrame:Inverse() * towPart.Position;

		rope.Length = (attachment.WorldPosition - rope.Attachment1.WorldPosition).Magnitude + 5;
		rope.Attachment0 = attachment;


		local targetDriverSeat = targetChassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');
		if targetDriverSeat then
			CollectionService:RemoveTag(targetDriverSeat, 'VehicleSeat');
			local seatWeld = targetDriverSeat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld');
			if seatWeld then
				seatWeld:Destroy();
			end;
		end;

		targetCar:SetAttribute('BeingTowed', true);

		local controls = car:FindFirstChild('Controls', true);
		if controls then
			controls:SetAttribute('Attached', true);
		end;

		plr.Character.Humanoid:UnequipTools();
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('_detachTow', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local car: Model? = plr.Car.Value;
		if not car then return; end;

		local rope: RopeConstraint? = car.Body:FindFirstChild('WinchRope', true);
		if not rope then return; end;

		local attached = car.Body.Bed:FindFirstChild('Attached');
		if not attached then return; end;

		local targetCar = GetCar(attached.Value);
		if not targetCar then return; end;

		local targetChassis = targetCar:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
		local targetPlatform: Part? = targetChassis.Platform;

		targetChassis.Mass.Massless = false;

		local targetDriverSeat = targetChassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');

		if targetDriverSeat then
			CollectionService:AddTag(targetDriverSeat, 'VehicleSeat');
		end;

		local originalOwner = targetCar:FindFirstChild('OriginalOwner');
		if originalOwner then
			local originalOwnerPlr: Player? = originalOwner.Value;
			if not originalOwnerPlr then return; end;
			if not originalOwnerPlr:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then return; end;

			if originalOwnerPlr.Car.Value == nil then
				originalOwnerPlr.Car.Value = targetCar;
				originalOwner:Destroy();
			end;
		end;

		targetCar:SetAttribute('BeingTowed', false);

		local controls = car:FindFirstChild('Controls', true);
		if controls then
			controls:SetAttribute('Attached', false);
		end;

		attached:Destroy();
		rope.Attachment0 = nil;
		rope.Length = 0;

		targetCar.Config.State.Hazards.Value = true;
	end)

	NetworkService.Connect('_winchIn', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local towTruck: Model? = plr.Car.Value;
		if not towTruck then return; end;

		local rope: RopeConstraint? = towTruck.Body:FindFirstChild('WinchRope', true);
		if not rope then return; end;

		local attached = towTruck.Body.Bed:FindFirstChild('Attached');
		if not attached then
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'You are not towing a car');
			return;
		end;

		if rope.Length <= 1.25 then
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'Winch is already fully retracted');
			return;
		end;

		local targetCar = GetCar(attached.Value);
		if not targetCar then return; end;

		if winchingIn[targetCar] then
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'Winch is already active');
			return;
		end;

		winchingIn[targetCar] = true;

        coroutine.wrap(function()
            while rope and rope.Parent and rope.Length > 2 do
                rope.Length -= 0.2;
                task.wait(0.08);
            end;
			winchingIn[targetCar] = nil;
        end)();
	end);

	NetworkService.Connect('_weldCar', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local towTruck: Model? = plr.Car.Value;
		if not towTruck then return; end;

		local rope: RopeConstraint? = towTruck.Body:FindFirstChild('WinchRope', true);
		if not rope then return; end;

		local controls = towTruck:FindFirstChild('Controls', true);
		if not controls then return; end;

		local attached = towTruck.Body.Bed:FindFirstChild('Attached');
		if not attached then
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'You are not towing a car');
			return;
		end;

		local car = GetCar(attached.Value);
		if not car then return; end;

		local targetChassis = car:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
		local targetPlatform = targetChassis.Platform;

		local weldStorage = Instance.new('Folder');
		weldStorage.Name = 'WeldStorage';
		weldStorage.Parent = towTruck;

		local carWeld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
		carWeld.Name = 'CarWeld';
		carWeld.Part0 = targetChassis.Platform;
		carWeld.Part1 = towTruck.Body.Bed.Main;
		carWeld.Enabled = true;
		carWeld.Parent = weldStorage;

		for _,v in next, targetChassis.Wheels:GetChildren() do
			local wheelWeld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
			wheelWeld.Name = 'WheelWeld';
			local wheelBall = v:FindFirstChildOfClass('Part');
			wheelWeld.Part0 = wheelBall;
			wheelWeld.Part1 = towTruck.Body.Bed.Main;
			wheelWeld.Enabled = true;
			wheelWeld.Parent = weldStorage;
		end;

		controls:SetAttribute('Welded', true);
	end)
	
	NetworkService.Connect('_unWeldCar', function(plr: Player)
		if not plr.Team == BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

		local towTruck: Model? = plr.Car.Value;
		if not towTruck then return; end;

		local rope: RopeConstraint? = towTruck.Body:FindFirstChild('WinchRope', true);
		if not rope then return; end;

		local controls = towTruck:FindFirstChild('Controls', true);
		if not controls then return; end;

		local attached = towTruck.Body.Bed:FindFirstChild('Attached');
		if not attached then
			_G.AeroError(plr, 'You are not towing a car');
			return;
		end;

		local weldStorage = towTruck:FindFirstChild('WeldStorage');
		if not weldStorage then return; end;
		
		weldStorage:Destroy();
		controls:SetAttribute('Welded', nil);
	end)
end


function TowTruckService:Init()
	NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
	Signal = self.Shared.Signal;
	WINCH_PREFAB = self.ServerAssets:WaitForChild('Winch', 10);
	GetPlayersWithinRadius = self.Shared.GetPlayersWithinRadius;
end


return TowTruckService

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/TowTrucks/WreckerService.lua ---

--[[
    WreckerService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → TowTrucks
    Parent: TowTrucks
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]

-- Wrecker Service
-- Khizzer
-- August 2, 2023

local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local Signal;
local NetworkService;
local CarService;

local UP_VERTICAL_C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.429145813, 3.45549393, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0.906307876, 0.422617942, 0, -0.422617942, 0.906307876);
local DOWN_VERTICAL_C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.429145813, 3.45549393, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0.970295727, 0.241921917, 0, -0.241921917, 0.970295727);
local TOWING_VERTICAL_C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.429145813, 3.45549393, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0.939692616, 0.342020154, 0, -0.342020154, 0.939692616)

local HOOK_SECTION_UP_C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.00392150879, -1.32622528, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, -1, 0, 1, 0);
local HOOK_SECTION_DOWN_C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.00392150879, -1.32622528, 1, 1.05598993e-07, 8.5512383e-08, 8.5512383e-08, -0.978147626, 0.2079117, 1.05598993e-07, -0.2079117, -0.978147626);

local RIGHT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1 = CFrame.new(1.20003986, 0.000190734863, 0.000385284424, 1, -8.74227766e-08, 0, 8.74227766e-08, 0.99999994, 2.98023224e-07, -2.48689958e-14, -2.98023224e-07, 0.99999994);
local RIGHT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1 = CFrame.new(1.20003986, 0.000190734863, 0.000385284424, -4.37113634e-08, 2.98023224e-07, -1, 8.74227837e-08, 1, 2.98023224e-07, 1, -8.74227695e-08, -4.37113883e-08);

local LEFT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1 = CFrame.new(-1.19995975, 0.000190734863, 0.000385284424, 1, -1.50995803e-07, 0, 1.50995788e-07, 0.99999994, 2.98023224e-07, -4.61852778e-14, -2.98023224e-07, 0.99999994);
local LEFT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1 = CFrame.new(-1.19995975, 0.000190734863, 0.000385284424, -4.37113883e-08, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0, -1, 0, -4.37113883e-08)

local BCAA_TEAM = 'British Columbia Automobile Association';

local WreckerService = {}

function WreckerService:_isWrecker(car: Model): boolean
    if not car then return false; end;

    local body = car:FindFirstChild('Body');
    if not body then return false; end;

    local boom = body:FindFirstChild('Boom');
    if not boom then return false; end;

    return true;
end

function WreckerService:Start()
    NetworkService.Connect('LowerWrecker', function(plr, interactionPart)
        local car = CarService.GetCarFromDescendant(interactionPart);
        if not car then return; end;

        if car ~= plr.Car.Value then return; end;

        if not self:_isWrecker(plr.Car.Value) then return; end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;

        if plr.Team.Name ~= BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Moving') then return; end;
        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Lowered') then return; end;

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Moving', true);
        local startTime = tick();
        local steppedConnection;

        local boom = plr.Car.Value.Body.Boom;
        local main = boom.Main;

        local firstAnimationSignal = Signal.new();

        local verticalWeld = main.VerticalWeld :: Weld;

        local initial = verticalWeld.C1;

        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3;
            if percent > 1 then
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                verticalWeld.C1 = DOWN_VERTICAL_C1;
                firstAnimationSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            verticalWeld.C1 = initial:Lerp(DOWN_VERTICAL_C1, percent);
        end);

        firstAnimationSignal:Wait();
        firstAnimationSignal:Destroy();
        steppedConnection:Disconnect();

        local hookAnimationDoneSignal = Signal.new();

        startTime = tick();

        local hookSectionWeld = boom.HookPivot:FindFirstChildOfClass('Weld');

        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3;
            if percent > 1 then
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                hookSectionWeld.C1 = HOOK_SECTION_DOWN_C1;
                hookAnimationDoneSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            hookSectionWeld.C1 = HOOK_SECTION_UP_C1:Lerp(HOOK_SECTION_DOWN_C1, percent);
        end);

        hookAnimationDoneSignal:Wait();
        hookAnimationDoneSignal:Destroy();

        local openClampsSignal = Signal.new();

        startTime = tick();

        local rightClampWeld = boom.Hook.RightClamp.Pivot:FindFirstChildOfClass('Weld');
        local leftClampWeld = boom.Hook.LeftClamp.Pivot:FindFirstChildOfClass('Weld');

        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 2;
            if percent > 1 then
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                rightClampWeld.C1 = RIGHT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1;
                leftClampWeld.C1 = LEFT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1;
                openClampsSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            rightClampWeld.C1 = RIGHT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1:Lerp(RIGHT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1, percent);
            leftClampWeld.C1 = LEFT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1:Lerp(LEFT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1, percent);
        end)

        openClampsSignal:Wait();
        openClampsSignal:Destroy();

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Moving', false);
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Lowered', true);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('ClampWrecker', function(plr, interactionPart)
        local car = CarService.GetCarFromDescendant(interactionPart);
        if not car then return; end;

        if car ~= plr.Car.Value then return; end;

        if not self:_isWrecker(plr.Car.Value) then return; end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;

        if plr.Team.Name ~= BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Moving') then return; end;
        if not interactionPart:GetAttribute('Lowered') then return; end;

        local boom = plr.Car.Value.Body.Boom;
        local hitbox = boom.Hook.LeftClamp.Hitbox :: BasePart;
        local clampFront = boom.Hook.Hook.ClampFront

        local overlapParams = OverlapParams.new();
        overlapParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {workspace.Cars};
        overlapParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Include;

        local parts = workspace:GetPartsInPart(hitbox, overlapParams);
        if #parts == 0 then return _G.AeroError(plr, 'No car found in clamp hitbox'); end;

        for _,v in parts do
            if v.Name == 'Wheel' and v.Parent.Parent.Name == 'Wheels' then
                local targetCar = CarService.GetCarFromDescendant(v) :: Model;
                local targetChassis = targetCar:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
                
                local name = v.Parent.Name;
                local frontOrRear = name:sub(6, 6);
                local leftOrRight = name:sub(7, 7);

                local otherWheelName = `Wheel{frontOrRear == 'F' and 'F' or 'R'}{(leftOrRight == 'L' and 'R') or 'L'}`;
                local otherWheelModel = v.Parent.Parent:FindFirstChild(otherWheelName);
                if not otherWheelModel then return; end;

                --The wheel it touched is v
                local otherWheel = otherWheelModel.Wheel;

                targetChassis.Mass.Massless = true;
                targetCar.Config.State.Hazards.Value = true;
                targetCar:SetAttribute('BeingTowed', true);

                local originalOwner;

                for _,v in next, game.Players:GetPlayers() do
                    if v.Car.Value == targetCar then
                        originalOwner = v;
                        v.Car.Value = nil;
                        break;
                    end;
                end;
        
                if originalOwner then
                    local original = Instance.new('ObjectValue');
                    original.Name = 'OriginalOwner';
                    original.Value = originalOwner;
                    original.Parent = targetCar;
                end;

                local targetDriverSeat = targetChassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');
                if targetDriverSeat then
                    CollectionService:RemoveTag(targetDriverSeat, 'VehicleSeat');
                    local seatWeld = targetDriverSeat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld');
                    if seatWeld then
                        seatWeld:Destroy();
                    end;
                end;

                local function WeldWheel(wheel: BasePart)
                    local weld = Instance.new('WeldConstraint');
                    weld.Part0 = wheel;
                    weld.Part1 = clampFront;
                    weld.Parent = clampFront;
                end;

                WeldWheel(v);
                WeldWheel(otherWheel);

                local clampFrontWeld = boom.Hook.Hook.Extension.ClampFrontToExtension;

                clampFrontWeld.Enabled = false;

                interactionPart:SetAttribute('Clamped', true);
                interactionPart:SetAttribute('Lowered', false);

                local steppedConnection;

                local raisedToTowSignal = Signal.new();
                local startTime = tick();

                steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
                    local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 2;
                    if percent > 1 then
                        steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                        raisedToTowSignal:Fire();
                        return;
                    end;
                    boom.Main.VerticalWeld.C1 = DOWN_VERTICAL_C1:Lerp(TOWING_VERTICAL_C1, percent);
                end);

                raisedToTowSignal:Wait();
                raisedToTowSignal:Destroy();
                break;
            end
        end
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('ReleaseClampWrecker', function(plr, interactionPart)
        local car = CarService.GetCarFromDescendant(interactionPart);
        if not car then return; end;

        if car ~= plr.Car.Value then return; end;

        if not self:_isWrecker(plr.Car.Value) then return; end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;

        if plr.Team.Name ~= BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Moving') then return; end;
        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Lowered') then return; end;
        if not interactionPart:GetAttribute('Clamped') then return; end;

        local boom = plr.Car.Value.Body.Boom;
        local clampFront = boom.Hook.Hook.ClampFront;

        local targetCar;

        local loweredDoneSignal = Signal.new();
        local startTime = tick();
        local steppedConnection;

        local clampFrontWeld = boom.Hook.Hook.Extension.ClampFrontToExtension;

        clampFrontWeld.Enabled = true;

        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 2;
            if percent > 1 then
                boom.Main.VerticalWeld.C1 = DOWN_VERTICAL_C1;
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                loweredDoneSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            boom.Main.VerticalWeld.C1 = TOWING_VERTICAL_C1:Lerp(DOWN_VERTICAL_C1, percent);
        end);

        loweredDoneSignal:Wait();
        loweredDoneSignal:Destroy();

        for _,v in next, clampFront:GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('WeldConstraint') then
                v:Destroy();
                targetCar = CarService.GetCarFromDescendant(v.Part0);
            end;
        end;

        if targetCar then
            local originalOwner = targetCar:FindFirstChild('OriginalOwner') :: ObjectValue;
            if originalOwner then
                if originalOwner.Value.Car.Value == nil then
                    originalOwner.Value.Car.Value = targetCar;
                    originalOwner:Destroy(); 
                end;
            end;
            local targetDriverSeat = targetCar.Chassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');
            if targetDriverSeat then
                CollectionService:AddTag(targetDriverSeat, 'VehicleSeat');
            end;
            targetCar.Chassis.Mass.Massless = false;
            targetCar:SetAttribute('BeingTowed', nil);
        end;

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Clamped', nil);
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Moving', false);
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Lowered', true);
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('RaiseWrecker', function(plr, interactionPart)
        local car = CarService.GetCarFromDescendant(interactionPart);
        if not car then return; end;

        if car ~= plr.Car.Value then return; end;

        if not self:_isWrecker(plr.Car.Value) then return; end;

        if typeof(interactionPart) ~= 'Instance' then return; end;

        if plr.Team.Name ~= BCAA_TEAM then return; end;

        if interactionPart:GetAttribute('Moving') then return; end;
        if not interactionPart:GetAttribute('Lowered') then return; end;
        
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Moving', true);
        local startTime = tick();
        local steppedConnection;

        local boom = plr.Car.Value.Body.Boom;
        local main = boom.Main;
        local verticalWeld = main.VerticalWeld :: Weld;

        local rightClampWeld = boom.Hook.RightClamp.Pivot:FindFirstChildOfClass('Weld');
        local leftClampWeld = boom.Hook.LeftClamp.Pivot:FindFirstChildOfClass('Weld');


        local clampsFoldedSignal = Signal.new();
        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            --Move the clamps to default
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 2;
            if percent > 1 then
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                rightClampWeld.C1 = RIGHT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1;
                leftClampWeld.C1 = LEFT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1;
                clampsFoldedSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            rightClampWeld.C1 = RIGHT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1:Lerp(RIGHT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1, percent);
            leftClampWeld.C1 = LEFT_CLAMP_UNFOLDED_C1:Lerp(LEFT_CLAMP_DEFAULT_C1, percent);
        end);

        clampsFoldedSignal:Wait();
        clampsFoldedSignal:Destroy();

        local hookSectionWeld = boom.HookPivot:FindFirstChildOfClass('Weld');

        local hookSectionRaisedSignal = Signal.new();
        startTime = tick();

        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 3;
            if percent > 1 then
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                hookSectionWeld.C1 = HOOK_SECTION_UP_C1;
                hookSectionRaisedSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            hookSectionWeld.C1 = HOOK_SECTION_DOWN_C1:Lerp(HOOK_SECTION_UP_C1, percent);
        end)

        hookSectionRaisedSignal:Wait();
        hookSectionRaisedSignal:Destroy();

        local verticalRaisedSignal = Signal.new();
        startTime = tick();

        steppedConnection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(function()
            local percent = (tick() - startTime) / 2;
            local initial = verticalWeld.C1;
            if percent > 1 then
                steppedConnection:Disconnect();
                verticalWeld.C1 = UP_VERTICAL_C1;
                verticalRaisedSignal:Fire();
                return;
            end;
            verticalWeld.C1 = initial:Lerp(UP_VERTICAL_C1, percent);
        end)

        verticalRaisedSignal:Wait();
        verticalRaisedSignal:Destroy();

        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Moving', false);
        interactionPart:SetAttribute('Lowered', false);
    end)
end;

function WreckerService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    Signal = self.Shared.Signal;
    CarService = self.Services.CarService;
end;


return WreckerService

--[[
    VariableMessageSign (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services → TrailerService
    Parent: TrailerService
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Variable Message Sign
-- Khizzer
-- February 1, 2023



local VariableMessageSign = {}

local NetworkService;
local FilterStringAsync;

function VariableMessageSign.ConnectEvents()
    NetworkService.Connect('SetTrailerSign', function(plr, trailer, text)
        if plr.Team.Name ~= 'Translink' then return; end;
        local signGUI = trailer:FindFirstChild('SignGUI');

        if not typeof(trailer) == "Instance" then return; end;

        if not signGUI then return; end;

        local signFilterResult = FilterStringAsync(text, plr.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);

        if not signFilterResult then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        local signTextFiltered = signFilterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();

        if not signTextFiltered then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        if string.find(signTextFiltered, '#') then
            _G.AeroError(plr, 'Text was filtered.');
            return;
        end;

        signGUI.SignText.Text = signTextFiltered;
    end)
end;

function VariableMessageSign:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
    FilterStringAsync = self.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
end;


return VariableMessageSign

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerStorage/Aero/Services/TrelloService.lua ---

--[[
    TrelloService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
-- Trello Service
-- Automationeer
-- August 7, 2023

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local TrelloService = {Client = {}}

local REFRESH_TIME = 240
local BAN_LIST_NAMES = { "Temporary Bans", "Permanent Bans", "Group Bans", "Ban List", "Group Ban List" }
local EXCLUDED_NAMES = {"Overflow Ban List", "Temporary Ban List", "____", "---", "------", "-------------------", "Group Ban List"}
local ADMIN_LISTS = {
  Creators = "HeadAdmin",
  HeadAdmins = "HeadAdmin",
  Admins = "Admin",
  Moderators = "Moderator",
}
local ID_BLACKLIST = {
  71812450, -- canuck
  84968930, -- bigred
  3079538820, -- brontols
  155362885, -- rovers
  5214110692, -- toxic_lz
  95769504, -- livelydad
  1705341800, -- opireto
  447596669, -- 123getajob
  217689796, -- jakeiscool
  113033187, -- bigred
  631317281,
  542718559,
}
local NAME_BLACKLIST = { -- lowercase
  ("canuckman77"):lower(),
  ("BIGREDOH4ISBOSS"):lower(),
  ("Brontols"):lower(),
  "r_overs",
  ("toxic_LZZZ0"):lower(),
  ("LivelyDad77"):lower(),
  "opireto",
  "123getajob",
  ("Jakeiscool7788"):lower(),
  ("THEBIGREDOH4"):lower(),
  ("BGZ93"):lower(),
  ("NaniMay1"):lower(),
}

local Trello = require(ServerStorage.Aero.Modules.Trello)
local trelloAPI = Trello("7b6cbc511dc1a5f6f7ebe68661c8a994", "ATTAc4c423264c9524606223d99ccf290f30db5b359526026ec36a2f7c8225034195D1270087")
local PlayerService

local function blankFlagData()
  return {
    ModBadge = { Usernames = {}, UserIds = {}, Groups = {} },
    Moderator = { Usernames = {}, UserIds = {}, Groups = {} },
    Admin = { Usernames = {}, UserIds = {}, Groups = {} },
    HeadAdmin = { Usernames = {}, UserIds = {}, Groups = {} },
    Banned = { Usernames = {}, UserIds = {}, Groups = {} },
  }
end
local FlagData = blankFlagData()
local lastUpdate = 0
local updating = false
local loaded = false

local function listInsert(tbl, entryName: string)
  if table.find(EXCLUDED_NAMES, entryName) then
    return
  end

  local split = string.split(entryName, ":")
  if split[1] == "Group" then
    local id = tonumber(split[2])
    local rank = tonumber(split[3] or -1) or -1
    tbl.Groups[id] = rank
  elseif #split == 1 then -- username
    if table.find(NAME_BLACKLIST, entryName:lower()) then
      return
    end
    table.insert(tbl.Usernames, entryName)
  else -- username:userid
    if table.find(ID_BLACKLIST, tonumber(split[2]) or 0) then
      return
    end
    if table.find(NAME_BLACKLIST, split[1]:lower()) then
      return
    end
    table.insert(tbl.Usernames, split[1])
    table.insert(tbl.UserIds, split[2])
  end
end

local function parseBanList(data, list, archive)
  local isTemp = list.name == "Temporary Bans"
  local cards = trelloAPI.Lists.GetCards(list.id)
  for _, card in cards do
    if isTemp and card.badges and card.badges.due then
      local date = DateTime.fromIsoDate(card.badges.due)
      if date and date.UnixTimestamp and date.UnixTimestamp < os.time() then
        if archive then
          trelloAPI.Request(trelloAPI.getUrl(`cards/{card.id}?idList={archive.id}`), "PUT", {}, {})
        end
        continue
      end
    end

    listInsert(data.Banned, card.name)
  end
end

local function parseAdminList(data, list)
  local cards = trelloAPI.Lists.GetCards(list.id)
  for _, card in cards do
    listInsert(data[ADMIN_LISTS[list.name]], card.name)

    for _, label in card.labels do
      if label.name == "Moderator" or label.name == "Senior Moderator" then
        listInsert(data.ModBadge, card.name)
        break
      end
    end
  end
end

local function doBoard(data, shortId, allowAdmins: boolean)
  local lists = trelloAPI.Boards.GetLists(shortId)
  local archive = trelloAPI.getListObj(lists, "Archived Bans")

  for _, list in lists do
    if list.closed == true then
      continue
    end

    if table.find(BAN_LIST_NAMES, list.name) then
      parseBanList(data, list, archive)
    elseif allowAdmins and ADMIN_LISTS[list.name] then
      parseAdminList(data, list)
    end
  end
end

function TrelloService:UpdateFlags()
  updating = true

  local ok, err = pcall(function()
    local data = blankFlagData()
	doBoard(data, "nWyWHruV", true) -- admin control board
	doBoard(data, "p1NEDGwq", false) -- ban control board

    FlagData = data
    lastUpdate = os.time()
  end)

  if not ok then
    warn("TRELLO FLAG UPDATE ERROR:", err)
    task.wait(20) -- lock everything for 20 seconds to give stuff time to breathe
    updating = false
  elseif ok then
    updating = false
    task.defer(function()
      local ok2, err2 = pcall(function()
        for _, player in Players:GetPlayers() do
          task.defer(PlayerService.HandleFlags, PlayerService, player)
        end
      end)

      if not ok2 then
        warn("TRELLO PLAYER UPDATE ERROR:", err2)
      end
    end)
  end
end

function TrelloService:SubmitJudicialCase(title: string, description: string)
	local lists = trelloAPI.Boards.GetLists("8Q0l6Ucp")
  local list = trelloAPI.getListObj(lists, "Unfiltered Submissions")
  trelloAPI.Lists.MakeCard(list.id, title, description)
end

function TrelloService:GetFlagData(yield: boolean?)
  if not loaded then
    if yield == true then
      if not loaded then
        repeat RunService.Heartbeat:Wait() until loaded
      end
    else
      return nil
    end
  end

  return FlagData
end

function TrelloService:Start()
  self:UpdateFlags()
  loaded = true

  RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if lastUpdate + REFRESH_TIME < os.time() and not updating then
      task.defer(TrelloService.UpdateFlags, TrelloService)
    end
  end)
end

function TrelloService:Init()
  PlayerService = self.Services.PlayerService
end


return TrelloService

--[[
    TrunkService (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerStorage → Aero → Services
    Parent: Services
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:53
]]
local TrunkService = {Client = {}};

local playerSessionStorage = game:GetService('ServerStorage'):WaitForChild('PlayerSessionStorage');

local NetworkService;

function TrunkService:Start()
    NetworkService.ConnectFunction('GetToolsInTrunk', function(plr)
        local tools = playerSessionStorage[plr.UserId]['Trunk']:GetChildren();

        local toolsToSend = {};

        for _,v in next, tools do
            table.insert(toolsToSend, {Name = v.Name});
        end;
        return toolsToSend;
    end)

    NetworkService.Connect('Trunk', function(plr, event, name)
        if event == 'Place' then
            plr.Backpack[name].Parent = playerSessionStorage[plr.UserId]['Trunk'];
        elseif event == 'Take' then
            playerSessionStorage[plr.UserId]['Trunk'][name].Parent = plr.Backpack;
        end;
    end);
end;

function TrunkService:Init()
    NetworkService = self.Services.NetworkService;
end;

return TrunkService;
